A. M. Maphumulo M. O. Mbatha

Amazwi okubonga 
Uma inkomo isigwaziwe yadindiliza phansi, isekelwa kahle em aceleni imiswe kahle ukuze ilungele ukuhlinzwa. Ngale nkathi kumele kubekhona ozoyatha kuhle komali wendima ensimini. Emveni kokuba seyathiwe, bayayithelekela-ke abahlinzi bayihlinze. Abahlinzi laba phela abakwazi ukuhlinza kahle bengekho abababambele izitho ezithile njengemikhono nemilenze. Ithi ingadatshulwa sekukhiswa okwangaphakathi, bese kubakhona labo abagqigqizelayo bekhama amathumbu abanye bechitha umswani. Inyama idliwa nje baningi abantu abasuke befake isandla ekuhlinzweni kwenkomo ize iyohlahlelwa iphekwe. Kuyenzeka-ke kwenye inkathi umhlinzi athande ukudideka kancane ukuthi konje izitho ezithile zikhishwa kanjani. Uma kuvela ukudideka okunjengalokhu, kuye kuqhamuke lowo mhlinzi onolwazi noma osakhumbula kahle ngesitho leso asize kuqhutshekwe kuze kuyophela. Kanti phela yini enye ngoba thina bendlu emnyama siphila ngakho ukuxhasana lokhu. 
Le nyama esigcwele izingqoko esiphambi kwethu, kubuye kwasiza laba abalandelayo ekutheni iphume kahle ngezitho zayo size siyiconsele namathe: 
* UMnumzane Vika Gabela ongumlolongi wamathwasa athwasela ukuchathazela ulwazi Iwemfundo kulabo abayomele. Lokhu kulolonga ukwenza eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu. 
* UMnumzane Bonginkosi Buthelezi okuthe isiya ngasekuhlahlelweni Ie nkomo wabe ephothula izifundo zakhe ze B. Com eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu. 
* UMnumzane Siphiwe 'Bhimbithi' Gumede osophikweni 
	lwakwa-Ndabazabantu 	emshinini 	ocwebisa 	ushukela 
eRossburgh, eThekwini. 
* UMnumzane Mfaniseni 'Komndane' Ntuli nengwevu yakwaMthiyane abasebenza nayo ekuxilongeni izimali ezikhokhela izinto ezithengwayo eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu. 
* Izintokazi ezibe yizindelabuthongo zahlala ezinkinobheni zemishini yakobeLungu zacofiya lezi zimpukane esesizibona zizinhle kangaka. Singeyilibale intokazi kaKhumalo okuyiyona ekhathule indima enkulu kulo msebenzi. Mbulazi!

Kubo bonke laba esesibabalile sithi Nime Njalo! Ningadinwa nangomuso. Siyethemba ukuthi nani amantshontsho eniwathole kulokhu kuhlinza ayothi noma emancane kodwa nindandanise nizame ukuwenza amavenge ukuze phela kusizakale nesizukuIwane esizayo. Lokhu ebesikwenza sibambisene' lapha, asikwenzeli thina kodwa sikwenzela isizukulwane esizayo ukuze leuthi noma isiyikhuthu Ie nyama bakwazi ukuyethula ethala bayidle basuthe.

1.1.1 Funda Ie ndaba bese uphendula imibuzo elandelayo 
Ukungcebeleka 
Uma ungayile emsebenzini noma esikoleni ngabe wenzani? Ziningi phela izindlela zokuchitha isikhathi. Abanye bethu phela isikhathi sokungasebenzi basichitha ngokuvakashela izihlobo nabangani kwezinye izindawo. Abanye ubafica behlezi befunda amaphephandaba kanti abanye kuye kuthi uma lishisa baziyele olwandle bayoshaywa umoya. Laba abaya olwandle yilabo abanenhlanhla yokuba seduze kolwandle. 
Umnandi kabi umoya oshaya olwandle ikakhulukazi uma liphu-. mile. Miningi imigilingwane eyenziwa olwandle lapha. Iningi Ialabo abasuke besolwandle lisuke lizibhukudela lizibusisa ngengubo yenhlanzi. Ukubhukuda kwasolwandle phela akufani nokubhukuda kwasemifuleni kanye nasezindaweni ezakhelwe ukubhukuda. Ulwandle lugubha amagagasi, amanzi alo awahlali athule nje. Lokhu kubikizela kwamanzi olwandle kwenza kungabilula ukushaya idadamu kuwo. Labo ababhukuda olwandle 
. basizwa ukuthi bade begwinja bevikana namagagasi. Abanye ubabona betshuza phezu kwawo amagagasi lawa beshona bevumbuka. Laba basuke betshuza ngokusamapulangwe okuyikhona kubenza bakwazi ukushona phansi babuye bakhuphuke namagagasi. Kanti kubhukudwa ngani phela ngoba kusuke kugqokwe ezakhona zokubhukuda ezihlala zithi ne emzimbeni. Bakhona nokho abanye oye ubafice bezibhushuzelela nje ngezingubo zangaphansi ezijwayelekile bangazifaki ezokubhukuda. Akubukeki khona lokhu kodwa-ke singebasole kakhulu nalaba ngoba phela nabo basuke befuna ukuzithokozisa. Kukhona abanye abalwesabisa okwenyoka ulwandle lolu. Bathi noma bezoshaywa umoya kulo kodwa bangacabangi nhlobo ukungena phakathi babhukude. Abanye-ke bathi uma befika olwandle bahlusule amahlamvu bawaphonse phakathi noma bakhiphe amaduku okufinya bawaphonse olwandle. Umuntu uye athi angaphonsa into yakhe emanzini, bese ema eyilinda ukuthi ibuye. Uma ingabuyanga phela kusho ukuthi naye uma eke wangen a emanzini ngeke abuye. Umuntu ongabuyelwanga utho lwakhe akalokothi nhlobo angene olwandle ngoba kuthiwa kungenzeka lumthathe luhambe naye. Abaziqamundayo-ke bathi abasokoco abalokothi nakancane ban gene olwandle. Singebaphikise nalaba abakhuluma kanjena. Amanye amanzi phela lawa. Wake wawabona amanzi athi emi ndawonye kodwa ebe ebikizela eya emuva naphambili. La manzi alungele bona labo abazishayelwa umoya abangazimbandakanyi nobubi.

Ubeka kanjalo-ke 10 ntanga. Awushaye ngezinqamulelayo-ke nawe usitshele ukuthi wenzani ngesikhathi sakho sokuphumula. Make sehlukane kule nkundla okwamanje siyobuye sihlangane ngokuzayo. 
1.3 Ukusetshenziswa kolimi 
Ukusetshenziswa kolimi kuveza izindlela ezehlukene umuntu angabeka ngazo lokho akukhulumayo. Kulo msebenzi owenziwa kulo nyaka lokhu kwehlukaniseke izigaba ezintathu. Kubalulekile ukuba sizisho siphinde sizichaze lezi zigaba. Lezi zigaba zilandelana kan jena: 
1.3.1 Izincazelo zamagama 
Izincazelo zamagama ziqukethe okuningi. Zikhombisa ikakhulukazi imigilingwane yolimi ekubekeni inkulumo ngezindlela ezehlukene. Ngaphansi kwezincazelo zamagama kungabalwa lokhu okulandelayo: 
Incazelo eqonde ngqo yegama isho into njengoba injalo. Incazelo ethe phecelezi isho ukubeka into ngenye indlela ube uqonde okunye. Lapha kusetshenziswa izinto noma izilwane ezithile ukumela lokho okusuke kuqondiwe. Uma sithi uThemba uyimvu, uyingwe, uyibhubesi, uyinkomo, uyinja noma uyimbuzi, siyazi ngempela lokho esisuke sikuqondile. Ngaphansi kwezincazelo zamagama sithola amagama anomqondo owodwa, aphikisanayo, akhomba ubulili kanye nalawo akhombisa izinto ezingena ngaphansi komkhakha othile. Okunye okubalulekile futhi lapha ukusetshenziswa kolimi olusankondlo olugudliselayo nangendlela yesimanje. Nokho kuningi okuwela ngaphansi kwa10 mkhakha. 
1.3.2 Ulwazi Iwamagama 
IsiZulu siwulimi olumtoti kakhulu ngokuba naniagama amaningi. Iningi lala inagama aseyizingane esiZulwini. Kukhona namanye amagama asaba amakhehla nezalukazi. Amanye amagama akhula ngesikhathi sawo, aguge emu va kwesikhathi afe agcine sesiwangcwabile. Lubalulekile ulwazi Iwamagama ngoba 
4 
Iwenza umuntu ukuba akhulume ngokukhululeka. Lwenza futhi ukuba umun'tu asebenzise igama okuyilona ukusho ngqo lokho asuke ekuqondile. Amagama ayizingane esiZulwini, ilawo ayimifakela eqhamuka kwezinye izilimi. Amagama asaba amakhehla kanye nezalukazi ilawo okuthuka njena esetshe~zlSlwe. Kukhona nalawo magama esingathi asefile, ngoba agclOa engasasetshenziswa nhlobo. 
1.3.3 Indlela yokusho okuthile 
Izincazelo zamagama kanye nolwazi Iwamagama yikhona okusiza umuntu ukuba abe nendlela yokusho okuthile. Kubonakala endleleni asho ngayo ukuthi uyajabula, uyabhinqa, uyancenga noma uthukuthele. Kunamagama amaningi athi uma esetshenziswe ngendlela ethile, aveze izimo. ezehluk.en~. Indlela yokusho okuthile ibuye ifake ukusetshenz,swa kohm. nge~dlela ethile. Lapha singabala ukusetshenziswa kwezaga kanye nez.sho. 
1.3.4 Awuphinde uzilhathe 
1. Shono izinhlobo ezimbili zezincazelo zamagama ezitholakala esiZulwini. 
2. Shono ezinye izinto ezintathu ezitholakala ngaphansi kwezincazelo zamagama. 
3. Nikeza umsebenzi wolwazi lwamagama. 
4. Shono ukuthi anjani amagama okuthiwa ayilokhu okulandelayo: 
	(a) Aseyizingane 	' 
(b) Asengamakhehla kanye nezalukazi (c) Asefile 
5. Shono okunye okungavezwa indlela yokusho okuthile. 
6. Shono izinto ezimbili ezisemqoka esiZulwini ezingena ngaphansi kwendlela yokusho okuthile.

1.4.1 Ukuguquka kwemisindo

1.7 Okudingeka ukuba kwenziwe 

Uthisha makaqedelise abafundi umsebenzi wesonto ongaqedwanga. Lokhu uthisha uyokwenza ngendlela ayibona ukuthi iyobalula kubafundi. Uma esezenelisile ukuthi uwuqedile, usengadlulela esahlukweni esilandelayo.

Isahluko 2 

2.1 Isivivinyo somcabango 




2.1.1 Funda Ie ndaba bese uphendula imibuzo elandelayo 
Ziyaphenduka 
"Hheyi wena ntombazane, ayifuneki imilenze emithathu lapha. Akuyona indawo yokuma lena, kuyasetshenzwa lapha," kusho induna ikhaea omunye okubonakalayo ukuthi ubesazihlabela ikhefana naye. Angen'zenjani umntanomuntu; yilokhu kusile ubaselwe yilanga. Nezintuli ezisuka khona azimnike thuba. Ubuye abuke nalezi zindadawe zamasimu kamoba. "Kade ugobile lapho wena kwenzenjani?" kubhoka induna ngesinye isankahlu futhi. "Ngiyaxolisa nduna bengiqinisa amaphathanisi ami lawa abesethanda ukuqaqeka," kuzikhalela elinye ibhungu elimtima sengathi likhuza umphezulu. 
Ngokukbuphuka kwemini nogalaweni abebelokhu bezihola phambili sebethanda ukukhenendeka. Ogalaweni phela abanakuzikhandla kakhulu ngoba akuwona iIlatasi 10 msebenzi. Ezansi ngasemfuleni kuzwakala upaniweli ehaya ingoma yakhe. Kuyezwakala ukuthi Ie ngoma uyihaya uza neno ngakulaba abakhuphezayo. Upaniweli yena uzwakala ekhululekile kunalaba ababhekene negeja. Kuwo lowo mnyama kusaeula upaniweli, 
nansi nensimbi yedina isishaya. 	' 
Sisuke esinamathambo wonke umuntu eseshiya phansi umsebenzi esephuthuma ukuyozisiza ngokuya ngasethunjini. 
Ngoshayile phela yilowo uqonda kulokho aziphathele kbona. Abanye baphatha imishumbu kanti abanye baphatha izixhafutini. Imishumbu lena igewala amahewu ajiyile kanti eminye ifakwa izititinya. Lapha ezixhafutinini uthola ukudla okunhlobonhlobo. Ezinye uzithola zinozolo oluthelwe umhluzi kwabekwa ihlo lenkomo ngaphezulu kanye nomdumba kapelepele. Sithi singaphela isikhathi sedina, kubuye kuphindelwe futhi okhuleni. 
Umoba lona phela uhlakulwa useyikhaba elineane. Akunakusukelwa umoba ongamahhohho kuthiwe uyahlakulwa. Uma kuhlakulwa-ke, ulapayi usondezwa eduze kwezithombo zikamoba. Umoba lona phela utshalwa ube imigqa emide ehamba ize iyofika ekupheleni kwensimu. Kuyenzeka eminye imigqa ibe ngotundu. Kodwa nayo lena iyahlakulwa. Lo msebenzi wokuhlakula umoba awuyona neze indobolo. 
Ziyaphenduka ngempela lapha emobeni kushikisha ufudu ngiyakutshela wena. Umuntu uma evela kohlakula umoba ulala angaphenduki.

2.2 Make sihlakule Ie nsimu yamaxoxo 
Makube yilo.wo nalowo lapha kithi bontanga asixoxele ngomseb~nzl owenzlwa kukhona indu~a ~qaphile. Masithi qaphuqaphu nJ~ bontanga slsho. ukuthl Ylmlphl Ie misebenzi eyenziwa kuqashlwe. OkubalulekIle. okufanele sikuthinte lapha ukuthi yimuphi ?gempela. u.msebenzl wend una, sikhona yini isidingo sokuthi t,!llsebenzl lbe nezinduna, izinduna osuwake wazibona wena zlbaph~tha ~anjani abantu. Omunye yena uma ekhuluma ngemisebenzl enezmduna ukhuluma kanje: 
"Izinduna mina se?gike ngazibona ziqaphe abantu uma kwenZl.wa Ie. mlsebenzl: kusetshenzwa emgwaqeni, kusetshenzwa kOJantshl, kwakhiwa izindlu kanye namabhilidi amakhulu kusetshenzwa emasimini ommbila. Engivamise ukukubon~ kulaba b~ntu abasebenza kukhona induna ukuthi bavamise ukubamblsana kakhulu nayo kangangoba uma kunamaculo aculw~yo aq~lwa yiyo induna Ie. Okunye engiye ngikunakisise ukuthl Ie mlsebenzl enezmduna imisebenzi umuntu ayenza ebheke inkokhelo kuyo." 
Sesizigeqile izigonogono ezindlebeni ntanga sesilindele wena ukuthi usithamundele sizwe. 
2.3 Indaba 
2.3.1 Indlela YOkuloba (izinhlamvu) 
Baningi abacabanga ukuthi ukuloba sebekwazi kahle-hIe' kanti akunJalo. Emtsebenzini eminingi elotshwayo maningi ama~hutha atholakal~yo. La ,!,~p~utha adalwa ukuthi abalobayo abanakek.eh, futhl abazazl lzmdlela ezamukelekile zokuloba. Sizo-ke slphawule ngezinto ezimbalwa okufanele uzazi uma uzoloba lSIZulu. 
12 
Amagama esiZulu ahlukaniswe ngezinhlamvu ezahlukehlukene. Uma kulotshwa amagama kusetshenziswa zona lezo zinhlamvu. Kuhle wazi kahle-ke ukuthi izinhlamvu zimi kanjani emagameni esiZulu. Iningi lithatha ngokuthi uhlamvu umsindo oxubanise ungwaqa nonkamisa kuphela. Onkamisa nabo bayizo izinhlamvu. Amagama esiZulu aqala ngonkamisa; agcine ngonkamisa futhi. Kuwo wonke la magama aqala ngonkamisa, osekuqaleni uluhlamvu. 
Ake sifunde 10 musho: 
Emasimini kudliwa uzolo. 
Amagama akule misho singawehlukanisa izinhlamvu zawo; kanje e/ma/silmilnil, kuldli/wa, ulzoflo. 
Okunye okufanele sikuqaphele uma siloba; ukuthi asilobi into efana ncamashi nalokho esikukhulumayo. Uma sixoxa noma sikhuluma ezinye izinhlamvu ziyeqiwa. Uma sesiloba zibhalwa zonke izinhlamvu nalezo esizeqayo enkulumeni. 
Amagama awasondelaniswa eduze kakhulu, futhi awaqhelelani kakhulu uma kulotshwa. Kufuneka kusale isikhala esilingene nje phakathi kwamagama. Umsebenzi olotshwe kwashiywa izikhala ezilinganayo phakathi kwamagama, uyathandeka futhi uyabukeka. Uma sibheka lapho kulotshwe khona ngomshini wokuthayipha, singabona ukuthi cishe izikhala phakathi kwamagama ziyalingana. 
Onke amagama ayisiZulu kuhle agcine ngonkamisa ngisho namagama asuselwe kwezinye izilimi imbala. 
2.4 Ukusetshenziswa kolimi 
2.4.1 Izinhlobo ezehlukene zezincazelo zamagama Incazelo yegama ekhombisayo 
Lolu hlobo lwencazelo yegama lukhombisa lokho okushiwo yigama njengoba kunjalo. Incazelo yegama ekhombisayo, kuye kuthiwe imaqondana noma iphathelene nokuthile. Incazelo yegama ekhombisayo, imayelana nencazelo eqondile yegama. Ngamanye amazwi singathi lolu hlobo lwencazelo yegama lumayelana nencazelo eqonde ngqo yegama. Incazelo yegama ekhombisayo singathi imayelana nencazelo eyisisusa yegama. Kwesinye isikhathi kungaqondiswa encazelweni eyisisekelo noma yangempela yegama. Uma sithi indlu sisuke siqondise kuyona

indlu, kungekho okunye esikushoyo. Lolu hlobo Iwencazelo lusuke Iuqondise kumqondo wento ethile. Lokhu kusebenza kakhulu ezinkondlweni. Kuyenzeka kwesinye isikhathi ukuba igama silithathe njengoba linjalo. Kwesinye isikhathi igama lingamela okuthile. 
Singasho kwesinye isikhathi okuthile, sithathela egameni elithile. Awubheke izibonelo: 
itshe-uyitshe 
inkomo iyahamba-uMandla uyinkomo ingulube-uyingulube 
Igama elithi itshe lisinikeza incazelo yegama njengoba injalo. Itshe ilokho okuqinile okuzivelelayo. Kepha uma sithi umuntu uyitshe sisuke sithi ulukhuni. Engaba uhlobo lomuntu okunikeza into emva kokuba usumncenge isikhathi eside. K wesinye isikhathi engakunikezi nhlobo. Kanjalo futhi uma sithi inkomo iyahamba, siqonde inkomo yangempela ukuthi iyahamba. Kepha uma sithi uMandla uyinkomo, kungenzeka ukuba siqonde ukuthi uyisiphukuphuku noma akakwazi ukudlala ibhola. Kanjalo negama elithi ingulube Iingasho yona Ie ngulube esiyejwayele, abayibiza ngokuthi umbhekaphansi noma ukotshi. Kepha uma sesithi umuntu uyingulube, siqondise ekutheni udla kakhulu noma akazinakekeli uyangcola kakhulu, Incazelo ekhombisayo yegama, singathi inokuxhumanisa okuthile. Lapha kuxhunyaniswa igama nobunjalo balokho okukhulunywa ngakho. Igama elithi indoda lisho owesilisa osemdala. Kodwa Iingasho kwesinye isikhathi umuntu omsiphasipha, of aka ibhulukwe noma ibheshu, onesibindi futhi onentshebe. Igama elithi imfundo ligxile kakhulu emfundweni kunokukhuliswa komntwana. Uma sithi uKhoza wathola imfundo kahle. Lapha siqonde ukutbi wafunda kusenemfundo engcono. Mhlawumbe wafunda i"RDY AL" kwazi bani.

2.6 Imibhalo 
2.6.1 Izinhlobo zamanoveli 
Kuzobalwa lapha izinhlobo ezimbalwa. zamaNoveli. Singabala lapha la manoveli alandelayo: Inoveli ngenhlalo yabantu. 
Lolu hlobo Iwenoveli luphathelene nalokho okwenzekayo empiIweni yemibla ngemibla yabanlu. Luphathelene ikakhulukazi nokuhlalisana kwabantu. Lolu hlobo lwenoveli luvama ukuqukatba usikompilo Iwabantu. Kwesinye isikhathi luqukatha imikhutshana ethile eyenziwa abantu. Kungaba inoveli ekhuluma ngokuthakatha njengalena kaShabangu ethi Bamngcwaba Ephila. Ziningi ezinye izincwadi zesiZulu ezimayelana nenhlalo yabantu. Cishe iningi lazo Iithinta inhlalo yabantu. 
1. Inoveli ewumlando 
Le noveli ivama ukukhuluma ngomlando othile. Imvamisa kuye kube umlando ngeqbawe elilbile noma ngamakbosi atbile ayebusa esizweni sakwaZulu. Enovelini ewumlando' kuvama ukukhulunywa ngesigameko noma ngezigameko ezithile eziphathelene nomlando noma impilo yenkosi ethile noma umuntu othile owayedumile emlandweni. Ziningi izincwadi zomlando esezibhaIiwe esiZulwini. Lapha singabala izincwadi zikaGwayi ezingamanoveli. Singabala incwadi ethi Bafa Baphela. Yekanini nalena ethi Shumpu. Singabala futhi lapha incwadi kaMsimang ethi Buzani KumKabayi. Sibale ekaDube ethi Insila KaShaka nekaBhengu ethi Ukhalalembube. Nokho zikhona nezinye izincwadi ezingamanoveli ezimayelana nomlando. 
2. Inoveli epbatbelene nenkolo 
Imvamisa lolu hlobo Iwamarioveli luye luthinte izindikimba eziphathelene nenkolo. Indikimba ethandwa kakhulu abalobi. i1ena yeBhayibheli emayelana nendodana yolahleko. Incwadi kaXulu ethi Indlalifa Engenasibaya ithinta yona Ie ndikimba. Nokho uXulu uyathanda ukubhala izincwadi ezipbatbelene nenkolo. Enye ayibhalile ilena ethi Uthando Lunje-ke. Awakandi kakhulu amanoveli esiZulwini aphathelene nenkolo. Nokho sengathi anganda. 
3. Inoveli eyisigameko 
Lolu hlobo lwenoveli luthinta isigameko esithile esisuke senzeke empilweni. Kungaba isigameko esithile, mhlawumbe impi noma izimpi ezithile. Incwadi kaNyanda ethi Ifu Elimnyama iwuhlobo 
16 
Iwencwadi emayelana nesigameko esithile. !thinta ik~khulukazi impi yesibili yomhlaba. Nokho akhona amanoveh ayllolu hlobo esiZulwini noma engandile kakhulu. 
Qaphela: Ziningi izinhlobo zamaNoveli ezikhona kepha lapha kuthintwe ambalwa njena. 
2.6.2 Vuka uzithathe 
1. Cbaza iNoveli emayelana nenhlalo noma impilo yabantu. 
2. Enjani inoveli okuthiwa ingeyomlando? 
3. Ayadingeka yini amanoveli aphathelene nenkolo esiZulwini?

3.1.1 Funda Ie ndaba bese uphendula imibuzo elandelayo 
Zimbi izinto 
"Lo mfana kade ngamtshela ukuthi akehlukane nokuhuqana na. mambawu uma ezoshayela imoto. Lolu tavatava asengene kulo angazi ukuthi ngizolwenzenjani. Usuke lana izolo sengimsola ukuthi amahabulo asethanda ukumeqa kanti usazodlula eshibhini, kwaGretta. Angazi ukuthi into engizoyithini lena," asho ani kine ikhanda uKhathide kubonakale ukuthi iyamudla Ie nto. "Mina malurne into engixakayo ukuthi kanti uma umuntu etholakale eshayela edakiwe useye avalelwe phakathi yini. Ithanda ukungiphica Ie nto eyenzeke kumzala uZenzele. Ebengikwazi mina ukuthi uma usolakala ukuthi usuphuzile, amaphoyisa ayakufuthisa . noma akuyise kudokotela akumome igazi. Ngiyakweshwama lokhu kokuvalelwa ngaso leso sikhathi utholakala emgwaqeni." 
Baxoxa nje oThulasizwe noninalume abamile iyasha imoto baphikelele esitokisini lapho kuvalelwe khona uZenzele. Sekuze kuthi ngesikade amphendule uninalume. "Phela mshana umzala wakho lona kuthiwa ubengaphuzele ukuphila. Imoto kuthiwa ibihamba igcwala umgwaqo. Bathi-ke abazwile kuthe abanye abashayeli uma bebona isimo esinje, bavele baphuthuma emaphoyiseni bayobika ngale mota ezodala ingozi emgwaqeni. Ezakwadalawane zimtice esayidansisa khona lapho emgwaqeni. Zimthathe zamjikijela ngemuva evenini imoto yashayelwa eHnye iphoyisa eseyovalelwa." "Awu malume kusho ukuthi bekukubi kakhulu baze bamphuce nemoto pho!" Kusho lokho mshana. 
Impela angiyazi indaba yentsha ukuthi sizoyithini uma ibulawa utshwala kanje. Into embi kakhulu owenu laba mshana abakwazi nokuphuza bazilinganisele bavele bathele umuthi enkomeni nje. Benjalo nje futhi mshana bakhonze lobutshwala obubi ugologo. Sengathi ungaqhubeka njalo wena nokungaphuzi. "OZenzele

baphuza umuntu bese ephenduka imfaduko nje," asho anxaphe. "Nakhu sesitike eshantshi mshana asehle." Nembala behle baqonde emnyango owawuphambi kwabo.

Asinkanti phela bontanga sishaya ngamafu~hi nje sithinte izihlokwana ezimqoka. Masikhule-ke b~ntanga slb~ abazali bese sibeka ukuthi singathandani nokuthi smgaxwayam ekukhuliseni izingane zethu. Umfundisi yena wode esishekelela nje uma kubonakala ukuthi siyaphambuka. Nanku umsebenzl esizowenza emakhaya wobonwa ngokuzayo: Utshwala sebuytbulele intsha yakithi.

3.3 Indaba 
3.3.1 Izimpawu zenkulumo 
Enye ingxenye esemqoka kakhulu ekulobeni; izimpawu zenkulumo. Abafundi abaningi abazi ukuthi izimpawu zisetshenziswa ngobuciko nangokunakekeJa okukhulu. Umsebenzi olotshiwe kodwa izimpawu zenkulumo azasetshenziswa, awufundeki kalulao Kwesinye isikhathi leyo nto esuke ilotshiwe ayizwakali kahle izimpawu zingekho. 
Kufanele uzazi izimpawu zenkulumo ezisetshenziswa uma kulotshwa. Ezinye izimpawu ezisemqoka, ofeleba, ukhefana (ikhoma) ungqi, umbuzi kanye nezinye. Uma kulotshwa zonke lezi zimpawu esizibalile ziyasetshenziswa. Okusemqoka wukuthi olobayo kufanele azi kahle ukuthi zisetshenziswa kuphi lezi zimpawu. Ezinye izimpawu zingasetshenziswa kaningi emshweni owodwa. 
Ofeleba ezinye zezimpawu ezisetshenziswa kakhulu uma kulotshwa. Ofeleba bayasebenza uma kuqalisa imisho, noma emagameni ezindawo nawabantu. 
Olunye uphawu olusemqoka ukhefana. Ukhefana usiza kakhulu ekuphumuzeni lowo osuke efunda lokho okulotshiwe. Kwenye inkathi ukhefana wenza ukuba umusho uzwakaie kahle umqondo wawo. 
Yonke imisho ekugcineni ivalwa ngongqi. Akukhethwa noma ngabe umusho mude noma umfushane kakhulu. Ungqi uyena okhombisa lapho kuphela khona umusho. 
Umbuzi uphawu olukhombisa ukuthi umusho lowo ungumusho obuzayo. Umuntu ofunda umusho obuzayo kufanele ezwe ukuthi umusho of una impendulo lowo. 
QapheIa ukuthi uma uloba uzisebenzise zonke izimpawu ngendlela efaneleyo. 
3.3.2 Thalha ezakho 
Faka izimpawu ezifanele kule ndatshana engezansi. 
Nifuna bani 10 muntu oboshiwe ubedakwe efile akalazi negama lakhe ngoba uthena unguzehlakalo eha akusiyena lowo esimfunayo.

3.5 Uhlelo 

3.5.1 Isiphawulo 

Isiphawulo wucezu olutholakala ngaphansi kwesichasiso. Umsebenzi omkhulu wesiphawulo ukuchaza usobizo emshweni. 

Ake sifunde Ie misho: 

Amaphoyisa amade ayasebenza. Imoto enkulu ishayisile. 
Umzala omdala uboshiwe. 

Kule misho engenhla amagama: amade, enkulu, omdala ayiziphawulo. Emshweni achaza amabizo. 

Isiphawulo sakhiwe ngezakhi ezimbili ezisemqoka. Lezi zakhi isi. vumelwano nesiqu. Isivumelwano isakhi esingasekuqaleni kanti isiqu singasekugcineni; kanje: 
	Isiphawulo 	Isivumelwano 	Isiqu 
	obubi 	obu- 	-bi 
	elifushane 	eli- 	-fushane 
	omkhulu 	om- 	-khulu 
	esisha 	esi- 	osha 

Isakhi esisemqoka esiphawulweni yiso isivumelwano lesi. Ake sibone ukuthi sakhiwa kanjani isivumelwano sesiphawulo. Ukwakhiwa kwezivumelwano zesiphawulo. 

Izivumelwano zakhiwa ngokuhlanganisa isakhi a. kanye neziqalo zamabizo, bese kwenzeka ukulumbana konkamisa.

3.6 Imibhalo 

3.6.1 Izinhlobo zamanoveli (ziyaqhutshwa) 1. Amanoveli ahlekisayo 

Lana ngamanoveli abhalelwe ukuba asihlekise. Kuvamise ukuba bawagxeke abafundi amanoveli alolu hlobo. Bathi abukeka enesi. sindo esincane uma eqhathaniswa namanoveli ayiqiniso asinikeza isithombe sangempela sempilo. Inoveli ejabulisayo nayo ingafakwa ngaphansi kwamanoveli ahlekisayo. Inoveli ejabulisayo inokuhlekisa ngabalingiswa ababambeke ezimweni ezinzima. Inoveli ehlekisayo ingaqukatha lokho okuhambisana nonya ngokuba ihlekise ngokwehluleka komuntu. Kuyenzeka kwesinye isikhathi ukuba inoveli ehlekisayo ibe nobuqiniso obuthile. Kwesinye isikhathi inoveli ehlekisayo ingahlekisa ngobuphukuphuku benlsha. Inoveli ehlekisayo inokubhinqa okuthile, izama ukuhlekisa ngokungaziphathi kahle kwabatltu. 
2. Inoveli efundisayo 

Lolu hlobo Iwenoveli luvama ukuthatha umlingiswa onenkani lumdlulise ochungechungeni Iwezinto ezimfaka esilinganisweni. Ekugcineni kwenoveli ilapho umlingiswa azithola khona ukuthi usekhulile ngengqondo. Kwesinye isikhathi uye athole okunye okuthile ngaye. Onke amanoveli aqala ngokuba. umlingiswa

oqavile abeyingane, ekhombise ukukhula kwalo mntwana aze abe mdale, lawo manoveli kuthiwa ayafundisa. Isibonelo inoveli kaNyembezi ethi Mntanami! Mntanami! 
3. Inoveli ngempilo yomuntu 
Lapha kuvama ukuba umbhali abhale ngempilo yakhe. Kwesinye isikhathi uchaza kusukela ngenkathi ezalwa, ekhula, eqala ukufunda kuze kufike lapho agcina khona. Engaqhubeka achaze nangenkathi efundela umsebenzi kuze kufike isikhathi sokuba aphumelele. Kwesinye isikhathi iphawule nangenkathi eqala umsebenzi, kanye nezinkinga ahlangabezana naw. Ingaqhubeka ibalule nangenkathi. umlingiswa lowo eshada, nezingqinamba abhekana naw empilweni yakhe yomshado. Isibonelo saloluhlobo lwenoveli ilena ebhalwe uMuntu Xulu ethi Mahlayalla! Mahlayana! 
4. Inoveli yothando 
Inoveli emayelana nothando ingaxoxa ngabalingiswa abathile abathandanayo; izingqinamba ababhekana naw kuze kufike esikhathini lapho beshada khona noma bevelelwa umshophi othile. Zikhona izincwadi eziyilolu hlobo esiZulwini. Inoveli kaKenneth Bhengu ethi uNyambose noZinitha inakho lokhu. Nokho azandile kakhulu izincwadi ezigxile othandweni esiZulwini .. 
3.6.2 Suka ezishozini 
I. Chaza kafishane ngenoveli ehlekisayo. 
2. Isuke injani inoveli okuthiwa iyafundisa? 
3. Chaza ngamafuphi okumayelana nenoveli ngempilo yomuntu. 
4. Chaza kafishane inoveli yothando. 
3.7 Okudingeka ukuba kwenziwe 
. Uthisha makaqedelise abafundi umsebenzi ongaqedwanga kule10 sonto. Uthisha uyolandela indlela abona ukuthi abafundi bayoyizwa kangcono uma eyisebenzisa. Uma esenelisekile ukuthi uwuqedile ngempela umsebenzi, usengedlulela emsebenzini olandelayo.

4.3 Indaba 
4.3.1 Ukuselshenziswa koleleba 
Sesike saxoxa ngokusetshenziswa kwezimpawu zenkulumo uma kulotshwa. Ezinye izimpawu ezisemqoka ofeleba. Ake sibhekeke ukuthi basetshenziswa kuphi ofeleba. Ofeleba basetshenziswa kakhulu uma kulotshwa amagama ezinto, abantu nezindawo. 
1. Onke amagama abantu asebenzisa uhlamvu oluwufeleba emva konkamisa oqalisayo, kanje: 
uMboniseni, uHleziphi, uKaMagagula, uNozidumo, uMaMbhele. 
3. Izinsuku zesonto: 
uMgqibelo, iSonto, uLwesihlanu. 
3. Esibiza ngakho abanye abantu: uMfundisi Mfeka, uMnurnzane Dlomo. 
4. Uhlamvu lokuqala lwesiqu luba ufeleba uma sibhala izilimi izizwe, amagama ezindawo, izinyanga kanye nezincwadi ezi~ seBhayibhelini, kanje: 
iNdiya, umXhosa, isiNgisi, isiPedi, kwaDukuza, eThekwini, ?Ndini,. uMeyi, uMasingana, uJulayi, amaHubo, uGenesisi, ,Zaga. 
5. Uhlamvu lokuqala luba ufeleba uma kubhalwa izihloko, amagama ezincwadi, namagama achaza izinto ezihlonishwayo namagama ezindawo, njengamaposi nezikole, kanje: Inkinsela yasemGungundlovu, Noma Nini, uMoya Ongcwele, ulwandle Olubomvu, Ongoye, Ohlange, KwaDlangezwa. 
4.3.2. Gadla sibone 
Lungisa Ie ndatshana ngokuloba izimpawu ezifanele: 
Safika ondini ngodisemba izulu lina. Umfula uthukela ugcwele uchichima. Umfundisi chonco wafunda encwadini kamathewu. Sasuka lapho salibhekisa kwanongoma. 
4.4 Ukusetshenziswa kolimi 4.4.1 Ziyini iz~ga 
Abantu abaningi izaga bazichaza ngezindlela ezehlukene. Isaga singamagama asetshenziswa mihla namalanga. La magama aqukethe ukuhlakanipha. kwabantu, ubunzulu kanye nokujula 
26 
kwezimpilo zabo. Izaga zingamagama okuthi uma esetshenziswa, alunonophalise ulimi luzwakaIe kamnandi. La magama adidiyele konke ukuhlakanipha, amaqiniso, ulwazinjula kanye nolwazinzulu lwabantu kanye nomphak'lthi. Kwesinye isikhathi izaga . ziqukatha uIimi Iwethunga'lwakudala. Izaga zivusa qingqo ulimi oludala oselwakhohlakala. Zivusa ulimi olwalukhulunywa oNdaba kanye noMalandela. Ngenxa yokunona kwezaga, kuthi cosololo ngisho kontembuzane uma sezisetshenziswa. 
Izaga zingamagama esiwajwayele, kodwa okuthi ngendlela asetshenziswe ngayo abe nokuyola okwemukeleka kubantu bonke ukuthi ngempela lana ngamagama ahlakaniphile. Zonke izaga ezikhona, noma ngabe zichaza okujabulisayo noma okudabukisayo; inhloso yazo enkulu ukufundisa. Iningi lazo lifundisa indlela okudingeka ukuba kuphilwe ngayo. Zifundisa ukuthi umuntu izinto azenzayo, akazenze ngokuhlakanipha. Zifundisa futhi ukuthi umuntu akabheke izigodi kanye nezingoxi angase akhalakathele kuzo empilweni. La magama ezaga athi uma esesetshenzisiwe kubonakale ukuthi aqukethe okuthile okuyisifundo. Ngale ndlela izaga ziba yincwadi empilweni yomuntu, ngoba kuningi akufunda kuzona. 
Izaga zivama ukuba yiqoqa noma zifinyeze izehlakalo zempilo yomuntu azifunde kanzima noma ngokudlala. 
Izaga zimbandakanya ndawonye ngamazwi ambalwa zonke izehlakalo zempilo. Ngenxa yokuthi izehlakalo zempilo zehlukene, nezaga kuze kube sengathi ziyaphikisana. Awubheke njena lezi 
•. . zaga ezilandelayo: 
"Vize uvalo, inqobo isibindi," kanye nalesi esithi "Kusinda ezakwaluvalwana. " 
Lokhu kuphikisana kwezaga kuveza ngokusobala ukuthi abantu izinto bazibona ngezindlela ezehlukene. Izaga ziyindlela yokufunda usikothi kanye nosikompilo Iwesintu. Izaga zikhomba ukuthi abantu baneso elibukhali kangakanani. Abantu babuka imikhuba yendalo ebazungezile njengezilwane izinyoni, imvelo 
I kanye nabantu abaphila nabo. Izaga zikhomba lokho abantu abakuthandayo, abakuzondayo, abakuhloniphayo kanye nalokho abakweyisayo. Kuzwakala emazwini abawasebenzisa ezageni ukuthi leyo nto bayithatha kanjani.

4.5 Uhlelo 
4.5.1 . Ukuselshenziswa kwesiphawulo 
Ziningi izindlela esingasebenzisa ngaso isiphawulo. Sivame ukusetshenziswa njengesichasiso noma njengesenzo. Uma sisetshenziswa njengesichasiso isiphawulo, sisetshenziswa nesivumelwano saso. Uma sisetshenziswa njengesenzo, kukhona umehluko omncane owenziwa esivumelwaneni sesiphawulo. 
Ukuze sibone kahle umehluko; akesisebenzise futhi isiphawulo emshweni. Kule misho engezansi, isiphawulo siyisichasiso: 
Umfana omdala akaphilile. Insizwa emfushane iyalobola. Uzibophe ngebhande elisha. 
Kwesinye isikhathi isiphawulo singasisebenzisa njengesenzo. Uma sisebenza njengesenzo, kweqiwa unkamisa oqalisayo esivumelwaneni sesiphawulo. Esigabeni sesihlanu, akeqiwa unkamisa kepha uguquka abe unkamisa i .. 
Ake sifunde Ie misho elandelayo: 
Amasokisi madala. Intombazane inhle. Umnumzane mkhulu. 
Kule misho engenhla; amagama, madala, inhle, mkhulu, ayisenzo esisuselwe esiphawulweni, kanje: 
	lsiphawulo 	lsenzo 
	amadaia 	madala 
	enhle 	inhle 
	omkhulu 	mkhulu

4.5.2 Zibambe ziqine 
Guqula Ie misho engezansi ibe nesiphawulo esiyisenzo: 
Intombazane enhIe, emva kokugeza ihambile. Umuntu omkhulu uma esekhaya lakhe. Izinkomo ezimbili ezifele edlelweni. 
Isikhathi esiningi uwena ongasebenzi. 
Indlu yakhe enkulu bayishisile. 
4.6 Imibhalo 
4.6.1 Isingeniso noma isichasiso senoveli 
Isingeniso seNoveli sivama ukuba sekhasini lokuqala. Leli khasi livama ukuqukatha lokhu esikubiza ngokuthi iskhasi~ noma isikhanyiso seNoveli. Isingeniso siyinto engesiyona INoveh kepha eyisichasiso. Kuyasiza ukuba inoveli uyizwe kahle. Isichasiso ku: dingeka sehlukane nalokho esikubiza ngokuthi i.noveIL Umlobl uye achaze into ezosisiza ekuqaleni kwenoveh. KW!SIChas!so kuvama ukwethulwa izingqinamba abalingiswa abazobhekana nazo. Kwesinye isikhathi kusetshenziswa inkulumompendulwano kusuke kwethulwa inkinga umlingiswa oqavile abhekene na~o okufuneka ayixazulule. Kwisichasiso umbhali usini~eza ulwazi oluthile. Lokhu kuyisingeniso noma isiqalo seNoveh, kusethulela abalingiswa nesimo ababhekene naso endaweni ethile. 
Isichasiso ekuqaleni kwenoveli sinikeza umfundi isendlalelo esi. dingekayo senoveli. Isichasiso sibeka uhIa lwezimo e.zitholakal~ ohlakeni Iwenoveli. Lezi zimo ezitholakala ohlakem Iwenoveh kudingeka ukuba zikhuliswe. Yisona isichasiso esisakhela umoya wenoveli. Yisona futhi esethula abalingiswa benoveli, sibuye sichaze ukuthombululeka kwezigigaba. Esichasisweni kuvama ukutholakala ulwazi olusemqoka olumayelana nohlaka kanye nezigameko ezisuke zizolandela enovelini. Kwesinye isikhathi umbhali wenoveli unikeza ulwazi echaza ngalokho osekuvese kwenzekile. Konke lokhu kungena ngaphansi kwesichasiso. Umbhali wenoveli ovelele uyakwazi ukwethula isichasiso ngaphandle kokuthikameza isenzeko senoveli, nangaphandle kokuthikameza ingxoxo yenoveli. 
29 






Okudinga ukuba kwenziwe umbhali wenoveli ngokushesha ekuqaleni kwenoveli, ukunikeza inkulumo eyisendlalelo edingwa abafundi ukuze bezwe isenzeko esizolandela. Umbhali 'wenoveli kudingeka asehlukanisele abalingiswa, asitshele ubudlelwano kanye nokuhlobana kwabo, bese esebhebhezelela umlilo wodweshu ngaphandle kokuchitha isikhathi. 
Ukuthi laba balingiswa bangobani nokuthi benzani, kudingeka ukuba kucace kusuka phansi njena. Izigameko eziba sesichasisweni, yizona eziye ziqalise inoveli. Kudingekile ukuba sazi ukuthi yini umbhali wenoveli aqonde ukuyichasisa. Ukuyisho. Umoya we nove Ii. Isendlalelo sabalingiswa. Uhlaka. Imifanekiso ethile. Indlela ethile abhala ngayo. Impendulo yalapha ukuthi umbhali akakuveze lokhu zisuka phansi njena.

Isiminyaminya 
"Ukuthula makube nani-Amen. Ukuthula makube naniAmen. Nginibingelela ngesibingelelo sendodana kaThixo eyabingelela ngaso abafundi. bayo. Lezi zindimbane zezimvu zikaBaba osezulwini eziphambi kwami, zingikhumbuza indodana kaThixo okwathi emveni kokubona isixuku sa bantu silambele ubomi baphakade, yabe seyenyukela entabeni yabashuinayeza. Mina-ke ngizibuka bese ngibuza kumninimandla onke ukuthi nginawo yini amandla okuhola lezi zimvu zakhe ukuziyisa embusweni waphakade. Ukuthula makube nani-Amen." 
Bathi uma bevuma u-Alnen, kuzamazame lonke leli qelekazi lalapha eMoriya. usukuiwesithathu lolu kwahlanganwa lapha. Kuhlanganwa minyaka yorke lapha eMoriya ngalesi sikhathi sonyaka ukuzovuselela imiphefumulo. Abantu bangangoZulu eya emakheni. Bafike ngezinhlobonhlobo zezinto zokuhamba. Amabhasi yona ayikhulunywa eyawo uhluleka ngisho ukuwabala. 
Usuku olukhulu namhlanje ngoba kukhona umsunguli waleli sonto. Phambili lapha endaweni ephakeme ukhangwa yizingubo ezimhlophe qwa kanye nemibhoshongo yezigqoko emakhanda. Imibhoshongo yezigqoko lena ayifani. Kukhona emikhulu kune-' minye kanti eminye igcwele ubucwebecwebe obusagolide. Ababhishobhi-ke laba bale mibhoshongo yezigqoko. Nabo phela abalingani, kukhona abakhulu kanye nabancane. Bonke bahlezi eduze kukababa wabo. Kunesikhulu isizotha lesi. 
Eduze kwababhishobhi kunemiphongolo yokufaka imali yomnikelo. Kukhona okufakwa kuyo imali engamaphepha kuphela, bese kubakhona okufakwa kuyo ewuhlweza. Sekuyanyamfuka nje imali kule miphongolo. Leli langa elibelesele alizwakali ikakhulukazi ngosuku Iwanamhlanje ngoba kunedlozi elikhulu lesonto.

5.6 Imibhalo 
5.6.1 Indikimba yenoveli 
Inoveli ephilile iba nakho okuthile esuke iqonde ukukudlulisela kumfundi. K wesinye isikhathi kuba umqondo othile umbhali asuke eqonde ukuwufundisa umphakathi. Indikimba ingathathwa njengomnkantsha wenoveli. Indikimba yiyona ngqikithi noma umongo wenoveli ovama ukuvezwa ngendlela eqondile noma ethe phecelezi. Indikimba ivama ukuba imbewu yenoveIi, into esingathi isuse phansi umbhaIi wenoveli yamenza ukuba abhale. Abanye indikimba bayibiza ngokuthi umnyombo wenoveli. [ndikimba singasho ukuthi iyinhliziyo yenoveli ngoba iyona 
. ephethe sonke isakhiwo senoveli. [ndikimba singayifanisa nesiza noma isanda senoveli. 
[nto ikakhulukazi esuke isuse umbhali wenoveli, singathi kusuke kuyilezo zinto azibuke zamjabulisa noma azibuke zamcasula. Indikimba ingumongo ophathelene nenoveli. Indikimba yenoveli iyakwazi ukusembulela iphinde isifihlele okuthile mayelana nenoveli. Iyakwazi ukukhanyisa lapho okuxaka khona, yenze izinto zixazululeke kalula. Kwesinye isikhathi ziba zining; izinto ezisuke zisuse phansi umbhali ukuba abhale. Ingakho sib a nezinhlobo ezimbili zezindikimba esingathi: 
1. Indikimba ebalulekile kanye 
2. Nendikimba engumthelela. 
Indikimba ivama ukuba umqondo ophethe inoveli. Umbhali wenoveli akabachazeli abafundi ukuthi usebhala indikimba yenoveli manje. Umfundi uzitholela yen a indikimba yenoveli emva kokuba eseyifunde wayiqeda. 
Indikimba yenoveli sifinyelela kuyona ngokuba sizihlaziyele la maphuzu alandelayo. Siye sihlaziye abalingiswa, uhlaka, umqondo wenoveli, ngisho isihloko sayo imbala. Indikifuba yenoveli iyinkulumo eyiqiniso noma egudliselwayo endabeni. Le nkulumo yenzeka esimeni esithile futhi ibe ithinta abalingiswa abathile. Indikimba yenoveli iminineka' emhlabeni esiphila .kuwona. Indikimba yiyona eyinjongo yombhali wencwadi. Ukuhluza indikimba yenoveli kufana nokucaba imvove yethambo. Uma usuyitholile indikimba yenoveli, uvama ukuba nokweneliseka.

Uhlaka Iwenoveli 

Uhlaka luwukuhlelwa, ukulolongwa kanye nokuthandaniswa kwezigigaba ezisenovelini. Uhlaka singasho ukuthi lulingisela isenzeko. Kusemqoka ukuba uhlaka IweNoveli lube nesiqalo, 

, iphakathi naphakathi kanye nesiphetho. Kudingeka ukuba konke " lokhu kube nokuxhumana. Uhlaka singasho ukuthi luyingxoxo 

ngezehlakalo ezigxile kakhulu kwisisusa senoveli. Uhlaka luyilokho okwenzeka enovelini, kanye nokuhlelwa kwezigigaba ezihlobene eziyirnbangela yokuba abalingiswa baziveze ubunjalo babo. 

:. Isingeniso senoveli yisona esethula isenzeko esizolandela. Isigaba sokuhlaselana yisona esiyisisusa sesenzeko. Isona lesi sigaba esikhombisa umlingiswa oqavile enodweshu okukuyena; enodweshu nabanye; enodweshu nezinto zemvelo noma nokuhlalisana nabantu. Emva kwalokho sifinyelela esigabeni lapho inkinga sekulukhuni ukuba ixazululeke. Uvuthondaba lona lusivezela izimo 

eziphikasanayo sezifinyelele esicongweni somzabalazo wazo . Ukuxazululwa kwezinkinga kusifikisa esiphethweni sodweshu. Isiphetho seNoveli yisona esiqeda isenzeko. 

Uhlaka kwarnanye amanoveli kuyenzeka ukuba luthathe impilo yonke yomlingiswa oqavile. Lapha lumthatha ezalwa, ekhula, enza okuthile empilweni, kuze kufike esikhathini sakhe sokufa. Kunabantu abaningi abangaziyo ukuthi igarna elithi "Uhlaka" liqharnuka kuphi. Leli garna lithathelwe kwelesiFulentshi elithi "complol" elisho ukubopha uzungu. Ukubophela umuntu othile uzungu noma into ethile kusho ukuhlela isenzeko esithile esizoba nemiphumela emihle noma emibi. Abacebi bozungu baye baxoxe ukut!}i yilowo nalowo muntu uzokwenza ntoni. Baye babophe futhi ukuthi bazokwenza nini lokho, nokuthi bazokwenza kanjani. Urna sebeqede ukuhlela konke lokho, babe sebehlela indawo lapho lokho beyokwenzela khona. Isahluko 7 

7.1 Isivivinyo somcabango 
7.1.1 Lapha ngezansi kunezigaba ezimbili ezidinga ukuxhunywa ukuze zakhe indaba. Zama ukuzixhuma lezi zigaba uzenze zikhiphe indaba ephelele. Inike isihloko Ie ndaba yakho. 
Ngiyamuzwa ukuthi unamandla yena 10 mlisa. Noma enamandla kodwa angiboni ukuthi angayimela Ie miphonso yami. Ngifike ngimuthi sika phansi, avike aze agoqane kanti angikho lapho ngizoyiphonsa ezimbanjeni .. 
. . . Kuthiwa ugulela ukufa 10 muntu enabe nilwa naye. Uvuvukele wonke umzimba 10. Akusaqondakali noma udla izihlungu yini kanti wena. Ngiyasola kuzodingeka kubekhona imizamo oyenzayo ngalokhu. 
7.2 Uhlelo 
7.2.1 Ukwakhiwa kwezivumelwano zesibaluli 
Esifundweni esingaphambili siphawule ukuthi isibaluli sakhiwa ngesivumelwano nesiqu. Isivumelwano yisona sakhi esisemqoka ngoba igama silibona ngaso ukuthi liyisibaluli. Ake sibone-ke ukuthi izivumelwano zesibaluli zakhiwa kan jani. 
Zimbili izindlela zokwakha izivumelwano zesibaluli. Indlela yokuqala yileyo yokuhlanganisa unkamisa a- kanye neziqalo zamabizo. Uma kuhlangene lezi zakhi, kwenzeka ukulumbana konkamisa. Uma isiqalo sebizo sinomankankana, uyeqiwa umankankana nonkamisa olandelayo.

7.3 Ukusetshenziswa kolimi 7.3.1 Ziyini izisho 
Izisho zithe ukwehluka ezageni ngokuthi zona ziyaguquguquka ngezinkalhi zesenzo. Kuvamise ukuthi amagama esiwaziyo ukuthi asho ukuthini, engakusho lokhu esiwazi ekusho, kepha esho okunye okuseceleni. Singathatha isibonelo sesisho esithi: Ukudla amabele. Lokhu akusho ngempela ukuthi umuntu uphilela ukudla amabele. Lokhu kusho ukuthi usaphila noma usawadla anhlamvana. Njengalokhu kwenza izaga, izisho zinonisa ulimi, inkulumo izwakale kamnandi. Izisho ziyizinkulumo ezimfishane. ezivame ukufaka izenzo ukusho lokho ezisuke ziqonde ukukusho. Izisho zingamagama asetshenziswayo ukusinekela izimo ezithile. Izisho zingachaza okuthile njengoba kubonakala kunjalo, noma kwesinye isikhathi zethule omunye umqondo oseceleni. Izisho

ziyizinkulumo zabantu basendulo othi uma usuzihlolisisa kahle ubane ukujula kwazo. Izisho zakheke ngendlela yazo zodwa. Izisho zisebenzisa izenzo kanye namabizo aguquguqula izincazela zazo. Izona izisho ezikwazi ukuba zidlulise umqondo othile, inqobo njena isekutheni leso sisha sisetshenziswa kangakanani umphakathi. 
Umqondo wezisho uvela ekwahlukaneni kwezinto ezisetshenzisiwe. ezinkulumeni zabanlu bakudala. Izisho ikakhulukazi zakheke ngendlela ethile eyenza ukuba incazelo yazo iguquke kakhulu kula magama esiwajwayele. Kuvamise ukuba isisho siqalise ngesenzo bese kulandela ibizo. 7.5 Indaba 
7.5.1 Izigalshana zendaba 

Esigabeni esingaphambi kwalesi safunda ngakulotshwa kwendaba. Okusemqaka wukuthi uma silaba indaba siyehlukanisa ngezigatshana. Lezi zigatshana nama zahlukehlukene kuhle zakhe indaba eyadwa. Imiqanda esezigatshaneni zendaba yakha indaba eyadwa ehlangene. 

Isigatshana ngasinye endabeni siba nomqondo owodwa ose. mqoka. Umqanda Iowa avela kulesa sigatshana, uzwakala ekuqaleni kwesigaba. Uma umqanda asesigatshaneni lesa usuwethuliwe, siyanwetshwa isigatshana leso ngokuchaza lawo mqando. Kwesinye isikhathi isigatshana leso singanwetshwa Ilgokuhalula izillto ezisemqoka kuleso sigatshalla. Ukunwetshwa kwesigatshana kuya ngahlaba Iwendaba esuke ibhalwa. Esigatshaneni lapha obhalayo uveza ubucika nekhona lanke lakubhala. rhela kufuneka ofunda isigatshana lesa ezwe yanke inta equkethwe kuleso sigatshana. Okuscmqaka-ke ukuthi abha. laya aveze ubucika emshweni ayibhalile esigatshaneni lesa. Kuhle asebenzise imisho em ide nemifishane. lngcano kakhulu imisho emifushane ezigatshaneni ngoba yenza umqondo usheshe uveIe obala. 

Ekulobeni izigatshana, kuhle sisebenzise ulimi olumnandi noluklasile. Amagama ayahlungwa kulotshwe lawo ashaya emhloIweni. Uma kuchazwa, akuchazwe into ihlale obala, nongakaze ayibone kube sengathi uyayazi. Izigatshana ezihlotshiswe ngezisha, izaga nezimo zokukhuluma zincomeka kakhulu. 

Zonke izigatshana kuhle zibe nomusho oyisiphelho. Lo musho yiwona okhombisaya ukuthi umqondo wesigatshana leso uyaphela.

8.4 Masixoxisane 
Kufika umbiko usesikoleni wokuthi umama wakho ugula kabi useze waphuthunyiswa esibhedlela. Sithathe ngamehlo engqondo usuke nathi emva kokuthola 10 mbiko uze uyosibeka esibhedlela lapho umthola zimbambile izinhlungu. 
Umfundisi uyobona yena ukuthi ethulwa kanjani la maxoxo. Kuyobakuhle nokho ukuthi sithole isikhashana sokuthi silungiselele la maxoxo ethu ngaphambi kokuba siwethule. 
Kuhle phela bontanga kuthi lowo othula amaxoxo ahambisane nesimo sento ayishoyo. Phatheka kabi lapho kukubi ngempela, umamatheke futhi uma sikhona isidingo salokho. 
8.5 Indaba 
. 8.5.1 Izinhlobo zezigatshana 
Sesike saphawula ukuthi uma kulotshwa indaba siyehlukanisa ngezigatshana. Yileso naleso sigatshana sinomqondo waso kodwa owakha indaba. Umqondo ovezwa isigatshana ngasinye usiza ukukhuphula indaba. 
Izigatshana endabeni azifani njengoba vele zitholakala ezindaweni ezingefani endabeni. Kukhona phela izigatshana ezingasekuqaleni kwendaba, kube ezisemzimbeni wendaba, nalezo eziyisiphelho sendaba. Izigatshana ezisemzimbeni wendaba ziba ziningana zona, ngoba yilapho olobayo esuke esegxila khona endabeni yakhe. Lezi zigatshana zomzimba 
	wendaba zingumongo wendaba yonke. 	n 
Kukhona isigatshana esisekuqaleni endabeni esibizwa ngokuthi isingeniso. Uma kulotshwa indaba asisali lesi sigatshana. Yisona phela esethula okuzoxoxwa ngakho kuleyo ndaba. Kusemqoka ukuthi obhalayo asenze sihehe isingeniso, futhi akhombise ukuthi uyasazi isihloko leso okulotshwa ngaso. Akukuningi okulotshwa esingenisweni, nokho kufanele siyingenise indaba ngendlela egculisayo. 
59 




74. 
75. 
Umzimba wendaba wakhiwa ngezigatshana ezindkudlwana kunesingeniso. Izigatshana lezo kuhle zibe nomqondo owodwa owendl~lekile. Lezi zigatshana zomzimba zinongwa ngolimi olumtotl namagama ekhethelo. 
Isigaba esiyisiphetho sendaba sincane n~so njengesingeniso. Olobayo esiphethweni usuke esekhombisa ukuthi usekusho konke obekungashiwo ngesihloko leso. 
8.5.2 Phum' ungibhule!! 
Bhala umehluko phakathi kwesigatshana esiyisingeniso nesiphetho. Ungeqisi emigqeni eyisithupha. 
8.6 Imibhalo 
8.6.1 Isenzeko senoveli 
Inoveli iba nesenzeko, isigameko okuyisona esenza ukuba indaba iqhubeke. Isenzeko siba usinga okuyilona oluthunga inoveli. Enovelini kuvama ukuba nento egelezayo eyenza ubundaba bendaba ukuba bufike esicongweni. Isenzeko isigemegeme esikuyona inoveli esiyenza ukuba ibizwe ngalelo gama. Isenzeko esitholakala enovelini ethile sehlnkene nesenzeko senye inoveli. Isenzeko isona esikhulisa inoveli. Umbiko noma isifundo enove- . lini kuvama ukutholakala kwisenzeko. Isenzekonhliziyo noma isigemegeme nhliziyo yisona esithunga uhlaka. Isenzeko sivama ukuba nala maphuzu alandelayo: 
1. Isenzeko sivama ukuba nesenzo esisenza sibhibhe. 
2. Sivama ukuba yingxubevange yokuthile okwenzekayo bese sigcina sesixaka. 
3. Amandla ayimithelela adala amandla okufa ukuba abe 
maningi lokho okugcina kudale inhlekelele. 
Isenzeko enovelini singahlukaniswa sibe izinhlobo ezimbili. Kukhona isenzeko esingaphandle esiphathelene nalokho okulingiselwayo noma okwenziwayo enovelini. Kukhona isenzeko sangaphakathi-esingathi uhlobo Iwesenzeko olwenzeka ezingqondweni zabalingiswa. Enovelini sikhonjiswa indlela imizwa yabalingiswa abehlukene echukuluzwa ngayo, nokuthi ixabana kanjani. Sikhonjiswa nokuthi imibono iphikisana kanjani. Kwesinye isikhathi sikhonjiswa ukuthi okungaphakathi ezingqondweni zabalingiswa kulwa kanjani. Kubalulekile ukuthi umbhali wenoveli aphumelele ukuba kubekhona ukuxhumana 
60 




kwesenzeko enovelini yakhe. Izenzeko kanye nemininingwane engayikhulisi indikimba yendaba, kwehlisa okushaqisayo kanye nokuxhumana kwenoveli. Isenzeko sibalulekile enovelini ngoba yisona inoveli eyakhelwe phezu kwaso. Ngaphandle kwaso inoveli ingeze yakhula ifike ezingeni eliphezulu. lsenzeko enovelini siveza abalingiswa ngezindlela ezehlukene. Abalingiswa kunesenzeko esithile abasenzayo esisemqoka enovelini. Isenzeko isona esikukhombisa ngempela ukuthi indaba izokhula ibheke ngaphi. Isenzeko singasho ukuthi kwasona ngokwaso siwumgogodla wenoveli. Ngaphandle kwaso inoveli ngeke yabakhona. 
8.6.2 Awugadle ngezakho 
1. Chaza ukuthi yini isenzeko. 
2. Nikeza amaphuzu amathathu avama ukutholakala kwi- 
senzeko senoveli. 
3. Nikeza izinhlobo ezimbili okungehlukaniswa ngazo isenzeko. 
4. Shono nokunye okungakhonjiswa isenzeko. 
5. Ungasho yini ukuthi inoveli yakhelwe phezu kwesenzeko? 
8.7 Okudingeka ukuba kwenziwe 
Utisha makaqedelise abafundi umsebenzi walelo sonto ongazange uqedwe. Uthisha uyozihlelela yena indlela eyovumelana naye yokwenza lokhu. Inqobo njena ukuthi akabe nesiqiniseko ukuthi abafundi bayawulandela umsebenzi.

Umahluko osobala ukuthi izivumelwano zesiphawulo zinomankankane, kanti ezesiphawulo azinabo omankankane.

Zikhona izivumelwano ezifanayo esiphawulweni nasesibalulini. Lezo ezifanayo umehluko ziwukhombisa kuphela uma zisetshenziswe neziqu zalolo cezu. Okusemqoka lapha ukuthi izivumelwano zesiphawulo zisebenza neziqu zesiphawulo kuphela. 
9.2.2 Ukwakhiwa kohlelo oluphikayo esibalulini 
Isibaluli siyakwazi ukuguqulwa sibe sohlelweni oluphikayo. Uma sakha uhlelo oluphikayo sisebenzisa isakhi sokuphika -nge-. Lesi sakhi sigaxwa phakathi kwesivumelwano sesibaluli nesiqu sesibaluli; kanje:

9.2.3 Nyakaza nyube! 
Kule ndatshana engezansi bhala phansi onke amagama anesivumelwano sesibaluli: 
Sabona ngomoya omakhaza ukuthi lizokuna. Laba abangenamajazi baqalaza. Okubuhlungu nje akekho noyedwa ongempofu kulaba bantu. Abaningi banamajazi ambalwa ampungana. 
9.3 Imibhalo 
9.3.1 Inkalhi enovelini 
Njengoba sazi ukuthi inoveli ingumfanekiso wempilo yangempela esiyiphilayo, kubalulekile ukuba impilo ifanekiswe ngesikhathi esithile esinikeziwe. Kubalulekile ukuba wazi ukuthi indaba yenzeka ngasiphi isikhathi. Kungabe yenzeka ekuseni, emini, ntambama noma ebusuku. Kufuneka uzame futhi ukuthola ukuthi umbhali ukhetheleni ukusebenzisa lezo zikhathi 
66 

enovelini yakhe. Kungabe indaba yenzeka ngenkathi lina liyidliva, noma ngenkathi libalele likhipha umkhovu etsheni. Inoveli kwesinye isikhathi ingaveza isikhathi samakhaza noma sokufudumala. Njengoba kuke kwashiwo ukuthi ukhetheleni umbhali ukusebenzisa !eyo nkathi, zibuze ukuthi bekungaba njani uma esebenzisa enye inkathi. Imvamisa kusuke kunesizathu esithile esisemqoka. 
Inkathi futhi ingakhomba inkathi yasendulo kanye nenkathi yamanje. Uma sikhuluma ngenkathi yasendulo, siqondise enkathini lapho imfundo kanye nempucuko yasentshonalanga ingakafiki. Zingakabibikho izinto zokuhamba abantu besahamba ngezinyawo amabanga amade. Zingakabibikho izinto ezifana nezingubo. Abantu besembatha izikhumba. 'Singabala nokunye okuningi okwakwenzeka ngenkathi yasemandulo. Izwe lisabuswa amakhosi kanye nezinduna. Kusekhona amabutho, kuhlala kuliwa izimpi. Enkathini yamanje singabala ukuthi sekukhona impucuzeko yaseNtshonalanga. Abantu sebefundile, sebenezimoto. Sebegibela nezindiza ukuvakashela abahlobo babo abathile. Esikhathini esiningi sebeshayelwa umthetho nguhulumeni. Noma inkosi inawo amandla, kepha amandla ayo awasefanani nalawo amakhosi ayenawo ngesikhathi sasemandulo. Kwakulula kuqala ukuba inkosi ikhiphe izwi lokuba kubulawe abantu. Nokho esikhathini samanje akusenjalo. Isigigaba noma izigigaba zenoveli kuyenzeka ukuba zenzeke ngenkathi engangosuku noma isonto. Singathatha njena isibonelo sokuthi inoveli emayelana nomshado kaThemba. Umbhali wenoveli ufuna ukusitshela isigigaba esibalulekile esenzeka ngosuku lwalowo mshado. 
9.3.2 Awuphinde uzilhalhe 
1. Chaza ukuthi inkathi iyini enovelini. 
2. Isiza ngani inkathi enovelini? 
3. Uma ucabanga umbhali usuke eyikhetheleni inkathi ethile enovelini? 

4. Chaza umehluko phakathi kwenkathi yasendulo kanye nenkathi yamanje. 
5. Shono ukuthi izigigaba zenoveli zibaluleke kanjani enkathini yayo.

9.4 Ukusetshenziswa kolimi 
9.4.1 Ukwenziwa isimanjemanje kolimi IwesiZulu 

Ulimi luye Iwenziwe isimanje ngokusebenzisa amagama amasha kulolo lulimi. EsiZulwini kunezindlela ezintathu zokwenza lokhu. Singabala lezi ezilandelayo: 
I. Amagama aqanjiweyo. 
2. Amagama atshelekiweyo. 
3. Amagama afanekiswe nolimi 1010. 
1. Amagama aqanjiwe 

Njengoba isihloko sizisho,. amagama aqanjiwe asho ukuqamba njena amagama amasha. Amagama amasha ayevamise ukuqanjwa ukuze kuqanjwe leyo nto entsha olimini IwesiZulu. Imvamisa kwakuye kubukwe ubunjalo bento ethile. Kwesinye isikhathi kwakuye kubukwe ukwenza kwento ethile. Kwesinye isikhathi kwakuye kubukwe ukwenza kwayo uma isetshenziswa. Ngaleyo ndlela izinto eziningi ezintsha zakwazi ukuba ziqambeke. Akutholakali ngempela ukuthi ubani owayeba nomsebenzi wokuqamba izinto ezintsha. Kusobala ukuthi kwakungumsebenzi womphakathi. 

lsibonelo 

Isibhamu saqanjwa kuthathelwa emsindweni waso uma siqhuma ukuthi sithi bhamu! 
Ugandaganda 

Isithuthuthu 

2. Amagama atshelekiwe 

Amagama atshelekiwe kuvama ukuba amagama athathelwa kolunye ulimi. Kwesinye isikhathi engathathelwa esiBhunwini, esiNgisini, esiFulentshini nakwezinye izilimi ezikhona ngaphansi komthunzi welanga. La magama aye elungiselelwe ukuba avumelane nesakhiwo samagama esiZulu. Izilimi eziningi zinamagama angagcini ngokamisa. Uma lelo gam a selenziwa isiZulu kuye kujotshelewe unkamisa ekugcineni. 
3. Amagama afanekiswe nolimi 1010 

Amagama afanekiswe nolimi oluthile kusuke kungamagama esiZulu asenomqondo othile wokwebolekwa kolunye ulimi. IsiZulu ikakhulukazi sivame ukuba siboleke esiNgisini noma

ngeniso.

ojalo.

Isahluko 10 
10.1 Isivivinyo somcabango 

10.1.1 Lapha ngezansi kunamagama afakwe ezibiyelweni. Amise kahle la magama wenze ukulhi avumelane nemisho levu akuyo bese uhlanganisa kahle Ie ndaba ngawo la magama nalawa angekho ezibiyelweni. 
Amankonyane (tshakadula) emva (ncela) konina. Phela kwakufanele ngoba (sutha) kwazise lonke ilanga (boshwa) ethombeni. Amaguqa wona (dushuza) onina (zama) ukuthi (ehlisa) ubisi. Yonke-ke imfuyo (klaba) emfundeni lapho (gcwala) enhle insinde Ie. Abelusi bezinkomo bona babethe chithi saka. Bebodwa (qwagela) kanti abanye (hlaba) uqhiwu (ciba) insema. (Khathaza) phela kakhulu imfuyo kwazise kwabe kuyisikhathi sasebusika. (Dla) amahlanga izinkomo kungekho lapho (ona) kuthiwe (ngena) ensimini zadla ikhaba lommbila. (Shona) ilanga abelusi (qoqa) izinkomo amabomb.o (bheka) ekhaya. Abanumzane phela (funa) izinkomo (valela) sekumnyama. Imfuyo (thi) kuhle ivalelwe esibayeni (bona) ukuze (bona) kahle yonke. Umfana (buya) imfuyo (mnyama) uvamise ukuthola idicane.

Indawo ebonakala ngamehlo ivama ukuthinta izindawo ezimaye. lana nomlando, izibonelo ENdondakusuka, EmGungundlovu, oPhathe nezinye izindawo ezibalulekile emlandweni. Indawo ebonakala ngamehlo ingafaka futhi izindawo ezithinta ukuhlali. sana kwabantu. Lapha kungathintwa indawo ekhuluma ngekhaya enovelini. Ikhaya liyisiqintana sezwe lokwehlukana ngemiqondo, lokuvumelana ngemiqondo, liyizwe lezenzo futhi liyizwe lokuthanda. Indawo ebonakala ngamehlo iqondise endaweni yangempela lapho okwehiakala khona izigigaba ezithile. Okubalulekile enovelini ukuthi indawo mayikholeke. Indawo isemqoka kakhulu kwisenzeko kanye nokuziphatha kwabalingiswa okwenzeka ohlakeni Iwendaba. Izindawo zibalulekile ukukhulisa indaba okukhulunywa ngayo. 

K wesinye isikhathi indawo ivezwa ngokusebenzisa lokho oku. khomba ukuthi ikhona. Uthisha nezingane angakhombisa ukuthi kukhona in dIu yokufundela okuthiwa isikole. Indawo ingakhonjiswa ngokuba igigiyelwe ingashiwo ngqo. Lokhu kungenziwa . ngokuba kukhonjiswe izindawo ngezinto ezenzeka kuleyo ndawo. Kungavele kukhonjiswe amasiko, ukugqoka, amancoko noma inkolo yendawo ethile. Umfundi usengazibonela ukuthi indawo . okukhulunywa ngayo ikwaZulu, iseMelika noma iseNdiya. Umlobi wenoveli uye angayisho indawo ukuthi ikuphi, kepha usebenzisa lokhu esikubiza ngokuthi ukusikisela. Indawo isinikeza ithuba lokuba sibone kahle lapho okwenzeka khona isenzeko, ibuye isize yandise lokhu esikubiza ngokuthi isenzeko. Indawo iyakwazi ukuba i1wise futhi ibuye ivikise abalingiswa. 

I yakwazi futhi ukuba i1ekelele abalingiswa kokuthile. Indawo kungenzeka kube yindawo yemvelo kanye nendawo yokwenziwa noma ekhandwa abantu. Uma sikhuluma ngendawo, sakhela abalingiswa izwe lapho bezohiala khona. Kwesinye isikhathi . indawo iba ummeleli, igcine ingasasho njena lokho ekumelele kepha isisho okungaphezulu kwalokho.

10.4 Ukuselshenziswa kolimi 
10.4.1 Ukudabuka kwezaga 

Izaga ziqanjwa ngabantu bebuka lokho abakubona kwenzeka empilweni. Lokhu kwenza ukuba izaga zivele ngezindlela ezehlukene. Kunezaga ezivela ezinganekwaneni. Lapha singenza isibonelo ngesaga esithi: Imbila yeswela umsila ngokulayezela. 

Ezinye izaga zivela ngalokho okuphathelene nenkolelo ethile yabantu noma usikompilo Iwabo. Kunezinto eziningi abantu abakholelwa kuzona. Ezinye zazo baye babone ukuthi uma ungazenzi zingase zilethe amashwa noma umshophi othile. 
Nasi isibonelo: Ungayishayi ingede ngoju. 
Ezinye izaga zivela emlandweni omdala wesizwe osuwakhohla

" kala. Umlando umayelana nezinto ezenzeka ngempela kepha osekunesikhathi eside zenzeka. Isibonelo salokho ilokhu okulandelayo: Amabonabonane ashiwo nguGcugcwa. 

Ezinye izaga zivela ezintweni ezindala ezenzeka eBhayibhelini kepha manje ezingasaziwa noma zake zenzeka. Lapha singathatha lesi sibonelo esilandelayo: Wahambisa okwejuba likaNowa. 

Ezinye izaga zivela ezintweni ezenzeka ngesikhathi samanje. Lapha singabala izinto eziningi. Nakhu okunye esingakuphawula lapha: Nopopo waze wabolela emthini uzithambisa. 

Ezinye izaga zivela ngendlela okubukwa ngayo amasiko ezinye ~zizwe. Kukhona izinto ezingenzeki nhlobo emasikweni ezinye IZIzwe: UmLungu angathunga isicoco.

10.6 Indaba 
10.6.1 Ukuhlangana kwezigalshana 

Noma indaba ilotshwa ngezigatshana ezahlukehlukene, kuhle kubekhona ukuzwana phakathi kwazo. Izigatshana zonke kufanele zibe nobudlelwano ukuze indaba ihlangane. Ukuhlanganisa izigaba kwenzeka ngesikhathi umuntu akha uhlaka Iwendaba. Ngesikhathi kwakhiwa uhlaka, imiqondo yendaba isuke ihlelwa, ngakho-ke nezigatshana nazo ziyahleleka. 

Izigatshana ezihleleke kahle zizwana, zenza ukuthi indaba ibe ne. miqondo elandelanayo. Yileso naleso sigatshana sithelelana nesinye. Akufanele kubekhona isigatshana esinomqondo ohluke kakhulu kweminye. Lokhu kungenza indaba ingahlangani kahle ifane nendaba ethathelwe phezulu engalungiselelwanga. 

Uma izigatshana zendaba zihleleke kahle zilandelana futhi zizwana; zakha indaba esheshe ibonakale ukuthi iqala kuphi ibheke kuphi. Umsebenzi omkhulu phela wezigatshana ukwenza ukuthi indaba izwakale isuka phansi ize iyofika emaphethelweni. Akwenzeki lokhu uma izigatshana zingalandelani ngononina. Izindaba eziningi zonakala khona lapha ekuhleleni imiqondo yendaba. 

Ukuze indaba yakho ibe nezigatshana ezihlangeneyo nezizwanayo, kusemqoka ukuba wakhe uhlaka indaba ungakayibhali. Uhlaka yilona olusheshe lukukhombise ukuzwana kwemiqondo nesakhiwo sendaba. Uma izigatshana zithelelana, futhi zisiza ekuqhubeni indaba, nakanjani uyobhala indaba ebumbene. 
10.6.2 Suk' ezishozini!! 

Ake ulobe ngamaphuzu angevile kwamahlanu ukuthi yini engakusiza ukuze ulobe indaba ehlangene.

Ukulumula 
Usana alunceli undendende nje. Luyayekiswa ibele noma ngabe unina unalo ubisi luningi. Lo muntu omncane akanakuncela nje phela angabe esama. Ukuyekisa ingane ukuncela kubizwa ngokuthi ukulumula. 
Ukulumula lokhu akwenziwa ingane ingakahambi. Kwenziwa ingane isihamba emveni kwesikhathi esiwunyaka noma esiwunyaka nesigamu. Ngale nkathi umntwana usuke esekwazi ukubona kahle abantu ahlala nabo. Yingayo phela Ie nkathi lapho esuke esekwazi ukukhulukhuluma amaganyana ambalwa anjengobaba nomama nokunye okunjalo. Ayilunyulwa neze ingane isencane kakhulu ngaphandle-ke uma kunezizathu ezithile ezingaba imbangela yalokhu. Lezi zizathu kungaba ukugula kukanina womntwana kumbe kube ukugula kwakhe umntwana engezwani kahle nebele. Esinye-ke isizathu kungenzeka ukuthi mhlawumbe unina usenzima. Izingane ezilandelana eduze ngale ndlela zibizwa ngokuthi amafumanankundleni. 
Umntwana-ke ulunyulwa ngokuthi kugcotshwe inhlaba ebeleni. Inhlaba Ie iyababa ngakho-ke ingane ithi iyancela izwe lokhu kubaba bese ikhala iba luqanduqandu. Kuye kubuywe kubulawe impukane kwenziwe izincwebana ziboshelwe entanyeni kuyo ingane. Lezi zincweba nazo kuthiwa zenza ukuthi ingane ingafuni ngisho ukulibheka ibele. Uma kwenzekile yathi iphuthaza ibele likanina, kuye kuthiwe phi bese iyayeka nayo ingabe isaqhubeka. Emveni kwesikhashana igcina isilikhohliwe impela ibele ingabe isahlupha nhlobo.

Ubisi Iwengane lubiza its he lemali, onina abazilumuli izingane masinya. Umzanyana ulungisa isitsha sephalishi, negula lamahewu ukuze uma sekomile okuyingane kuphuze. Ukubaba kwenhlaba kwenza ingane iluzonde ubisi Iwebele.

11.3 Imibhalo 
11.3.1 Uheho enovelini 

Kufuneka ukuba Iowo ofunda inoveli abe nezikhathi lapho asha. manqeka khona elokhu elingoza ukuthi kazi yini ezokwehlakala. Kufanele lowo olingozayo athinteke yilokho okungase kwehlakale. Uheho yilona olukhulisa inoveli luyifikise. kuvu.thondaba noma kwipholavuthondaba. Emva kwalokho moveh aYIsab.e isakhula kepha iya ngokubihlika. Igcina isiz~ yafika kulokhu eSIkubiza ngokuthi ibohlololo. Uvuthondaba Yllona olwe~z~ ukuba kuphele i1ukuluku umbhali wenoveli asuke ehsebenzlstle uku
thatha imiqondo yezibukeli. 
Inoveli kubalulekile ukuba ibe noheho oluya oja~o ngokukhul~' , futhi lwenze umfundi ukuba akhungatheke. Inoveh engal~landeh 
lolu khondolo idamane ifaka izenzeko eziyimithelela ezmgaha- , mbisani nenoveli. Lokhu kwenza umfundi ukuba aphelelwe umdlandla wokuqhubeka nokufunda inoveli. Kubalulekile ukuba izigigaba zenoveli zilamane kahle, zakhe uheho oluya .ngokukhula luze lufike entshakeni. Akufuneki ukuba umbhah afake

yonke imfucuza endabeni ngoba lokho kubulala uheho kususe nomqondo walowo ofundayo endabeni. Azifuneki izigigaba ezintantayo ojena, ezingasizi ngalutho ekukhuliseni uheho kanye nobumnandi benoveli. Alufuneki uhehombumbulu enovelini. Singakubeka ngokusobala ukuthi uheho luyisimo esisuke singasaqondakali kahle kungasaziwa mbhantshi ukujiya. Lapho imidlinzo isuke isithe bhe sekukhona ukucabangela kanye nosikisiki lokwazi okucashile ngenoveli. Umbhali wenoveli ongungoti ilowo okwazi ukuthunga inoveli yakhe ngosinga loheho, kusukela esingenisweni senoveli kuze kuyofika ekugcineni kwayo. 

Isibonelo esihle senoveli enoheho ileyo ebhalwe ngu D.B.Z. Ntuli ethi Ngiyoze ngimthole. Lapha uNtuli uyalukhulisa uheho ngokuba enze uGwaqaza ukuba engatholakali. UGwaqaza ufunwa uBhakubha kanye namaphoyisa. Uma bembuza kubantu, kuthiwa kade edlula njena khona manje. Lokhu kwenza ukuba umfundi elokhu edonsekile efuna ukwazi ukuthi kazi bogcina bemtholile yini uGwaqaza. Kubalulekile ukuba umbhali wenoveli kubekhona lokho asigodlela khona. Njengakuyo Ie ndaba uNtuli usigodlela ukubanjwa kukaGwaqaza kuze kufike ekugcineni.

11.5 Kwaphinda futhi lokho 
Namhlanje bontanga sizoqophisana ngalesi sihloko esilandelayo: 
Kuhle ukuthi ingane incele ibele likanina kunoma incele ubisi lwebhodlela. 
Umfundisi makaqembule ikilasi amaqembu amabili. Kula maqembu amabili masizikhethele amalungu amahlanu eqenjini ngalinye okuyiwona ezosimela. Elinye iqembu malivumelane nalesi sihloko kanti elinye maliphikisane naso. Umfundisi makabe umqaphi wala. maxoxo aze ayophela. Kodingeka umfundisi ancome lapho kuncomeka khona aphawule amaphutha kulabo abawenzile. 
11.6 Indaba 
11.6.1 Ukwakhiwa kwezigatshana 
Sesike saphawula ukuthi umuntu ozoloba indaba kuhle aqale enze uhlaka. Lapha ohlakeni uloba imiqonjwana emfikelayo ngaleso sihloko asinikeziwe. Leyo miqonjwana yiyona phela eha yizigatshana zendaba. 
Izigatshana zakhiwa zisuselwa emqondweni owodwa omkhulu. Lo mqondo wethulwa umusho wokuqala lapha esigatshaneni. Lo musho wokuqala singawuthatha njengesingeniso sesigatshana ngoba yiwona owethula okuzokhulunywa ngakho kuleso sigatshana. Umusho wokuqala esigatshaneni ulandelwa imishwana enweba yandise isigatshana leso. 
Imisho yonke elandela owokuqala esigatshaneni, isukela emshweni oyisingeniso. Nayo leyo misho elandelayo kufuneka izwane, ihambelane nomusho oqalisayo esigats!Ianeni. Lokhu yikhona okusiza ukunweba isigatshana leso. Imisho elandela owokuqala yiyona ecacisa, yengeze lokho okwethulwe umusho oyisingeniso sesigatshana. 
Izigatshana zifuna ubuciko obuthile ukuze umqondo lowo eziwuvezayo ukhanye ubesobala. Enye indlela yokwandisa isigatshana eyokusebenzisa amaqiniso odwa. Kwesinye isikhathi isigatshana 
83 




90. 
91. 
92. 
93. 
leso ungasinweba ngokubeka izibonelo nezehlakalo ezesekela umusho osekuqaleni. Uma uzosebenzisa izibonelo, qikelela ukuthi zizwana kahle nomusho oyisingeniso saleso ~igatshana. Ukuze izigatshana zakho zigculise endabeni, kuhle nazo uzakhele uhlakana lwazo. 
11.6.2 Ayihhashi!! 
Loba amaphuzu angeqile kwayisithupha ngokwakhiwa kwezigatshana. 
11.7 Okudingeka ukuba kwenziwe 
Uthisha makabukezise abafundi wonke umsebenzi owenziwe kulelo sonto. Uthisha uyozihlelela ngendlela abona ngayo indlela yokukwenza kangcono lokhu. Kudingeka uthisha abe nesiqiniseko sokuthi indlela ayisebenzisile iyavumelana yini nabafundi. Uma uthisha esenesiqiniseko sokuthi abafundi sebeyawazi umsebenzi, sekungaqhutshekelwa phambili.

12.1 Isivivinyo somcabango

94. 
95. 
96. 
12.1.1 Yipha amehlo kule ndaba uyifunde kakhulu ubuye uyifunde bulhule bese uphendula imibuzo elandelayo. 
Ukusina 
Ukusina lokhu igama eliqoqela ndawonye izinhlobo eziningi ezi. wukugida kwesiZulu. Kwakuyiyona disco yethu yomdabu kusadliwa ngoludala. Ziningi izinhlobo zokusina ezabe zikhona. Sizozama ukuthatha izinhlobo ezimbalwa sikhulume ngazo lapha. Uma kukhona ukusina okwaziyo wena esingakuthintanga lapha, uxole ngoba kuningi kakhulu ngeke sikuqede konke. Okunye-ke futhi phela kwehlukene ngezigodi. 
Indlamu: Indlamu ukusina okwimziwa ngokushaya kakhulu phansi okungaba okomuntu oyedwa noma kube iqembu labantu. Uma kusinwa kuyiqembu labantu, kushaywa kanyekanye phansi kubekhona ukudlisela ngornzimba. Kubhekwa ezindaweni ezahlukene. Yikhona kusina okujwayelekile lokhu. Nayo-ke indlamu lena yahlukahlukene. Nazi ezinye izinhlobo zendlamu esinazo: 
1. Isishameni: Isishameni ukusina okuhlanganisa umqhuqhumbelo kanye nendlamu ejwayelekile. Ungathi umuntu uyaqhuqhumbeia, uyambona useshaya indlamu futhi khona lapho. 
2. Isizingili: Ukusina lapho kuhlelembiswa khona iqolo kube nokunyakaza komzimba okuningi kubuye kushaywe kakhulu phansi. 
Olunye-ke uhlobo Iwendlamu olukhona yilolo okuthiwa isiBhaca. Lolu hlobo-ke lona luqhamuka ngapha ezansi nelaseNatali. 
Isigekle: Lokhu ukusina okwenzelwa endlini kuzungezwe iziko. Isigekle asifani sona nendlamu ngoba akuphuthunywa kakhulu ukushaya phansi. Kushaywa kanyekanye phansi kodwa kube nezikhawu kungaphuthunywa eduze. Kubakhona abakhombayo ababizwa ngokuthi izinkombi. Kudinga amaciko ukukhomba lokhu. Lona okhombayo umbona eshona evumbuka ngomzimba. Ngenkathi ikhomba inkombi, lab a abanye bona basuke beshaya izandla beqhilikisa imizimba kun jeya. 
Umqhuqhumbelo: Lokhu ukusina okwaqhamuka' nezintombi noma abesifazane abasheshe banqakela phezulu ukholo. Uma 
86 


kuqhuqhumbelwa, kushaywa ngezinyawo kulandelaniswe eduze kudlaliselwe nangernzimba. Izibukeli zishaya izandla ezihambisana nokuhlala konyawo phansi .. 
Umgqigqo: Lolu wuhlobo lokusina lapho kucwilwa khona ngemizimba kushonwe phansi naphezulu kuyiwe phambili kubuye kuhlehlwe kuyiwe emuva. Abantu besifazane abavamise ukwenza lolu hlobo lokusina. 
Umchwayo: Uma kuchwaywa kushoniswa imizimba phansi kube sengathi kuyahlalwa bese inyakaziswa iyiswe macala onke. Kuhlatshelelelwa phansi kube nokundonda. 
Inkondlo: Noma ingena .ngaphansi kokusina n je inkondlo; kodwa ithi ayihluke kancane ngoba yona iyiculo. Lapha ingeniswa ukuthi vele iyiculo eliculwa bese kuyasinwa. Leli culo lihaywa intombi ezogcagca. Iyihaya inkondlo yayo iphuma esibayeni kubo ibuye iyoyihaya futhi esigcawini ngelanga lomgcagco. Intombazane egcagcayo iyihlaba inkondlo isine iqephuze. Phela isuke isisina okukugcina ngoba isiphuma okokuphela ebuntombini. Uthi angayihlaba, bese zenanela nezinye izintombi asine aze akhombe ngesinqindi sakhe. 
Okusemqoka okumele singakulibali phela ukuthi kuthi kusinwa kube kuculwa. Yilolo nalolo hlobo lokusina luhamba neculo elivumelana nalo.

12.2 Uhlelo 
12.2.1 Ukwakhiwa kongumnini 

Esifundweni esiphambili siphawule ukuthi ongummm unezinhlobo ezimbili zeziqu. Ezinye zalezi ziqu yilezo zongumnini osuselwe kwezinye izingcezu. Ziningi izingcezu esingazishintsha 
zibe ongumnini. 	. 

Ongumnini angasuselwa noma angakhiwa ngamabizo. Lapha kuguqulwa ibizo libe ongumnini. Uma kuguqulwa ibizo liba ongumnini, siphongoza ngesivumelwano songumnini emabizweni bese kwenzeka ukulumbana konkamisa.

12.2.2 Shaya ngizwe bol 

Kule ndatshana engezansi tomula onke amagama angongumnini usho ukuthi asuselwe kuziphi izingcezu: 

Olunye uhlobo lwendlamu esinwa izingane zalowo mama. Uzifica zishosha okwesele lentaba, imilenze yazo ziyicothozisa kancane. Zasinela izinsizwa zenkulu iNkosi zancanywa. Abantu basemaphandleni ukudla kwabo phela indlamu. 
12.3 Imibhalo 
12.3.1 Udweshu enovelini 

Udweshu lusho ukushayisana kwemicabango ephikisanayo. Udweshu uma umuntu selumnkonkoshele akabe esazi ukuthi makenze njani. Udweshu lungafaka ukuqhudelana okuthize pha. kathi kweqhawe lendaba kanye nembangi. Udweshu luyisixakaxaka esibangela ukuthi izithandani, abangane kanye neziWobo zihlomelane izilimazo zize zigcine sezibhokodene ngemikhonto. Udweshu kuyenzeka ukuba lube ngaphandle. 
, K wesinye isikhathi udweshu luba ngaphakathi lapho esibona khona umlingiswa edwengulana futhi eshukana nonembeza kanye nemicabango yakhe. Udweshu lusho. ukungqubuzana kukanembeza nogovana kanye nokucinana okuphakathi enhliziyweni. 

Udweshu kujwayelekile ukuba lube phakathi komuntu nomuntu. Kwesinye isikhathi udweshu lungaba phakathi komuntn kanye nendalo. Okunye ukushayisana kuvama ukuba phakathi komuntu nesiko noma kukanembeza nogovane. Udweshu kwesinye isikhathi kuyenzeka ukuba lube phakathi komlingiswa nezimo ezithile. Mhlawumbe umlingiswa othile akafuni ukuzimbandakanya nornzabalazo. Ngenxa yokuthi uzithola sekunguyena yedwa ophikisana nokwenziwayo, ugcina ephoqelekile ukuba azihlanganise nawo. 
89 
98. 
1. 

1. 
99. 
100. 

Udweshu lungachazwa njengokushaqeka okulethela ubuhlungu okubangelwa ukungqubuzana phakathi kwalokho okuphikisanayo noma okuphambanayo kumuntu ngaphakathi. Lokhu kuphikisana kudalwa izifiso, isazela esithile, ubuqotho, inkolo kanye nokuziphatha kahle. Umgogodla oyinhliziyo yanoma isiphi isenzeko kanye nohlaka, yilona kanye udweshu lolu. Udweshu lusho ukungqubuzana phakathi kwabalingiswa abangezwani noma idlanzana labalingiswa. Kwesinye isikhathi kungaba ukulunga komlingiswa osemqoka kuphikisana nalokho adalelwe khona noma nesimo senhlalo. Kwesinye isikhathi ukushikashikeka noma ukutikatikeka kungaba phakathi komlingiswa kanye nengxenye ethile yobuyena. K wesinye isikhathi kungaba ukungqubuzana .phakathi komlingiswa nokululutheka kobuqotho bakhe. 
Njengoba sachaza ukuthi kukhona udweshu Iwangaphandle nolwangaphakathi; udweshu Iwangaphandle lungaba phakathi kwezindlela ezehlukene zempilo noma abantu abeWukene. Udweshu lwangaphakathi lungaba umshikashika ophakathi kumuntu, kuze kube sengathithi ulwa nobuyena ukuze azuze okuthize. Kukhona kwesinye isikhathi lapho umlingiswa elwa khona neminjunju kanye nobuthakathaka bakhe. Ngenxa yokuthi udweshu lusuke luyinto ephehlwe umuntu, kubalulekile-ke ukuba umuntu alukhombise kumuntu.

12.4 Ukusetshenziswa kolomi 

12.4.1 Isakhiwo samagama kanye nezincazelo 

Lapha sizobalula umsebenzi owenziwa izakhi zamagama. 1sakhiwo segama yisona esikwazi ukushintsha incazelo yegama. Siyakwazi ukunikeza incazelo yesakhiwo segama ngokuba sithole umsuka wegama. Uma sesiwutholile umsuka wegama siye 

90 





sibheke iziphongozo kanye nezijobelelo ezisetshenziswe egameni. Lokhu yikhona ngempela okusifikisa encazelweni yegama. Ngokubuka incazelo yegama elethwa iziphongozo kanye nezijobelelo zegama, siyakwazi ukwehlukanisa izincazelo zamagama izigatshana eziningana. Akesibheke njena ukuthi isiphongozo uku- singanikeza izincazel0 ezingaki ezehlukene: ukuhleka. ukuhlekisa, ukuhlekana 
ukuhlala, ukuhlalela 
Uma sibheka la magama angenhla, siyathola ukuthi kunokugudluka kwezincazelo zamagama okubangwa iziphongozo kanye nezijobelelo ezisemsukeni wegama. Akesithathe nanti igama eliyibizomuntu elithathelwa esenzweni -thunga. 
Kulesi senzo uma sesifaka: 
isiphongozo + umsuka + isijobelelo 
um- 	+ thung- +-i 
Lesi senzo esithi -thunga siphenduka ibizo umthungi. 1zincazelo zamagama zihamba zize zifake ukugudluzwa noma ukugudluka kwezincazelo zawo. Ukugudluka kwezincazelo zamagama kungenzeka ngalezi zindlela ezilandelayo: 
19ama elithi inWoko lingasho ikhanda. Kepha uma usuthi 1nhloko yesikole, usho ukuthi umuntu ophethe isikole. 
Kukhona namanye amagama avela kwamanye ngenxa yokusebenzisa izakhi ezithile. Akesithathe nanti elilandelayo: 
-hlola/umhlolil-hlolima. 
Enye indlela yokwenza izincazelo ezintsha zamagama, ukusebenzisa amabizongxube. Amabizongxube ayakwazi ukuveza amagama anezincazelo ezintsha: 

Uvelabahleke - vela + hlika Uvelakudlalwa - vela + dlala 
1ncazelo enye entsha yegama ingavela ngokuba kuphindaphindwe igama. Akesibheke njena lapha: Egameni elithi ikhanda singenza ibizomuntu elithi, umakhandakhanda.

12.5 Awuzilike ngengevu 
Namhlanje make silinganise ukwenza Ie misebenzi elandelayo: 

1. Ukuhlanza izingubo kusukela usazicwilise ensisheni (lokhu abakubiza ngokuthi ukusokha) zize zome zishiswe nge-ayini. 

1. Ukusebenza engadini ususa ukhula ubuye uchelele nezithombo ezikhona. 

Le misebenzi phela bontanga yenziwa abantu abehlukene emakhaya. Kukhona eyenziwa amantombazane bese kubakhona eyenziwa abafana. Masiyehlukaniselane-ke bontanga Ie misebenzi, kubekhona abethu abalinganisa ukuhlanza izingubo kanye nalabo abalinganisa ukusebenza engadini. Masiyilinganise Ie misebenzi kube sengathi sesiyayenza impela. Masikhuzane bontanga lapho sidideka khona kodwa sizimisele ngokuyenza lemisebenzi size siyiqede. Sizobuye sizitike futhi ngengevu ngokuzayo. 

12.6 Indaba 12.6.1 Isiphelho 

Ekugcineni indaba iba nesigatshana esiyisiphelho. Sifishane lesi sigatshana ngoba okuningi akushiwo kuso ngaphandle kokuphetha indaba. Siyisigatshana esisemqoka isiphetho ngoba yisona esikhombisayo ukuthi indaba iphela lapha. Indaba engenaso isi. phetho ayinambitheki kahle, kuba sengathi inqanyuliwe. Indaba engenasiphetho kuba sengathi iyekwe phakathi ingakapheli. 
Isiphetho sendaba kufuneka sibe nobudlelwano nendaba yonke. Umsebenzi wesiphetho wukuqoqa yonke imiqondo elotshwe ngesihloko esinikeziwe. Isiphetho siba sihle uma sikhombisa ukuzwana; nobudlelwano nesingeniso. Ekulobeni isiphetho kufanele kuqashelwe ukuthi singelulwa kakhulu ngoba lokho sekungayona futhi indaba. 

92 





Ingqikithi yesiphetho ukubeka imibono yakho wena olobayo. Imibona leyo nokho kufanele ihambelane nendaba. Olobayo angagxeka noma atuse lokho abekuloba mayelana naleso sihloko. Umuntu ofunda isiphetho kuhle ezwe ukuthi usesemaphethelweni endaba. 
Ake silobe isiphetho senye indaba lapha ngezansi njengesibonelo. Isihloko sendaba sithi: Uhambo ngesitimela. Isiphetho sale ndaba singafundeka kanje: 

Uhambo lwangalelo langa angikalukhohlwa. Zonke izigigaba nezehlakalo zalo zide zibuya kimi ngisho nasemaphusheni. Ukuba ngiyakwazi ukuzenzela ngabe ngizobuye ngiluqale phansi lolu hambo. Kuhlupha nje ngoba sekubiza imali ebomvu ukuhamba ngesitimela. 
Kulesi siphetho esingenhla kuneane esikushoyo, kodwa nokho kukhona ukuzwana phakathi kwesiphetho nesihloko. Kusho ukuthi isiphetho siyezwana nendaba yonke. Siyezwakala futhi lesi siphetho ukuthi akusaqhutshekwa nendaba, sekusongwa konke obekushiwo endabeni. 

12.6.2 Shaya ngizwe bol 

Fundisisa kahle Ie ngxoxo eyenziwe ngesiphetho ngenhla bese ubhala isiphetho sendaba enesihloko esithi; Ukuhamba ngetekisi. 

12.7 Okudingeka ukuba kwenziwe 

Uthisha makaqedelise abafundi umsebenzi walelo sonto ongaqedwanga. Uthisha lokhu uyokwenza ngendlela evumelana naye kanye nabafundi. Uma uthisha esezenelisile ukuthi umsebenzi uwuqedile, usengedlulela phambili.

Ukhukhuva 
Babezokhija ebusuku inyanga nodibi lwayo. Kwabe kungukhukhuva Iwenyanga elugaqasana kuhle komuntu owagwinya ucingo. Kwakungekhona ukungcamba komuntu lokhuya kwakuyisimanga. Wawungeke uhambisane nayo enyathukweni ngaphandle uma uzovele ukhenke uqobo lokukhenka. 
Lwathi lungaqeda ukunkiba udibi, Iwase luthatha umhlanti Iwakbija. Yayikhashana indawo ababeya kuyo ngakho-ke nalo Iwaphatha umbazo walo Iwawuxhawula nobhoko Iwase luma isibindi. Phandle lapha kwakumlima Ie nto eyinqaba. Wawuthi ungaphuma emkhathekweni, ungabe usabona nolunci. Umhlauti wawusumi ngomumo usulinde umkhapheyana Ion a ukuthi awugaxe zlye nawo. 
Phela undlela zinuka imiswani lona wayekade egingqe enkulu intondolo ngayizolo ewumncamo walolu hambo Iwabo. Izulu lalithanda ukuthwala. Lesi simo sezulu sasizobaphoqa ukuthi babuye bakhulekele isikhundla sokulala enyathukweni. Lalithi uma lishaya umbani izulu, zibonakale izimeshe zihlwabula esibayeni. Udibi lolu lwase luthanda ukuba nengebhekodwa ingekho into olungayenza ngoba phela isosha lifela emsebenzini walo.

13.3 Ukusetshenziswa kolimi 
13.3.1 Ukuchazwa kwezisho (kuyaqhutshwa) 

Izisho zingumthombo wolimi. Izisho zehlukile ezageni. ng~ba zona ziyaguquguquka ngeukathi yesenzo. Amagama eSlw~zlYO nesijwayele ukuwasebenzisa asinikeza incazelo ethe phecelezl. 



,) 

lzibonelo 

, Ukushaya ngesithende. Ukubamba inkunzi. 

Lezi zisho azisho ngempela ukushaya ngesithende lesi sonyawo kanye nokubamba inkunzi ngezimpondo. Incazelo yazo ijulile ngempela futhi ithe phecelezi kulena ejwayelekile: 

Ukushaya ngesithende- Ukushiya into, ungabe usazihlanganisa nayo. 

Ukubamha inkunzi- Ukuthatha into yomuntu ngenkani. 

Izisho zakha, zinothise ziphinde ziluhlobise ulimi. Ziyiqoqo lamazwi asebenzisa izenzo ukusho lokho ezisuke ziqonde ukukushoo Izisho zisetshenziswa lapho kuchazwa ubunjalo bezimo ezithile ngokusebenzisa umqondo osobala noma umqondo ocashile. Incazelo yezisho ayitholakali kalula, ngakho-ke zidinga ukuthi zicutshungulwe kuqala. Izisho zisebenzisa izenzo namabizo ukwedlulisa umqondo eziwuquketheyo. Ziyinkulumobuciko esebenzisa okwezaga kanye nemfumbe. 

Izisho zakheke ngendlela eyenza incazelo ishinlshe kakhulu kula magama esiwejwayele. Imvamisa isisho sigqamisa isenzo kuqala esiphongoze isiqalo uku-. Ibizo yilona elisinikeza incazelo yesisho. Izisho eziningi zikhombisa indlela esabizo. Ukusebenza kwezisho kuncike emishweni ezisebenza kuyona. Izisho ziwuhIobo oluthize Iwenkulumobuciko olukhombisa ukunotha kolimi. Ulimi luwulimi ngezisho. 

Ubuhle bezisho buvela kahle lapho zisetshenziswa emishweni. Izisho ziyinsika ephase impilo yomuntu. Ziyisinwe esivelele esintwini. Zinokujula okunomlando nenkambo engayiwa. Ulimi luba wulimi ngenxa yezisho. Ziyeluleka, ziyafundisa futhi ziqondise. Izisho zisebenzisa amagama ezinto esikwazi ukuzibona ngamehlo, ukuzizwa ngezindlebe, ukuzinambitha ngolimi, ukuzihogela ngamakhala kanye nokuzithinta ngezandla zethu. Izisho ziyindlela enhle ruthi emnandi yokusho into.

13.4 Uhlelo 
13.4.1 Ongumnini okhanyisayo 
Ucezu ongumnini lusetshenziselwa ukukhombisa ubunikazi. Kodwa kwesinye isikhathi luyachaza, lapho-ke akuveli yena umnikazi. Lolu hlobo longumnini silubiza ngokuthi ongumnini okhanyisayo. Lusivezeia indlela okusetshenziswa ngayo ongumnini. 
Ongumnini angakhombisa uknthi into yenziwe ngani: 
Umhlanti wesikhumba Isigqoko sotshani Ingilazi yephepha 
Ongumnini angachaza isikhathi oknsetshenziswa ngaso into ethile: 
Intondolo yokuncama Ijazi lokuhlinza Isigqoko sokwelapha 
Ubnlili bungachazwa ngongumnini: 
Abantu besimame Ibhubesi lenkomazi Imbuzi yensikazi 
Ongumnini angasetshenziswa uma kufanekiswa: 
Inyanga Ie wuqhotho Iwekhehla. 
Isagila esiphathwa udibi yikhanda lengane. 
Ongumnini uyasetshenziswa ukuchaza ukuthi into ethile isebenza ngani: 
Ekhaya kukhona isitofu samalahle. 
Inyanga igunda ngomshini kagesi. 
Akusashiswa izingubo ngensimbi yamalahle. 
Uyasebenza ongumnini ukuchaza okuphethweyo: 
Inyanga iphethe isikhwama semithi Udibi lugeza ibhodlela lamafutha Bakhanyisa ngedosha likamentshisi 
98 




Ongumnini angakhombisa ukulandelana kwezinto: 
Ukhukhuva lokuqala. Umuthi wokugcina. Isonto lesithupha. 
Ongumnini ofingqiwe emabizweni: 
Kwesinye isikhathi ongumnini uvela emabizweni njengesijobelelo. 
Lokhu kwenzeka emabizweni angombaxambili. Ongumnini uba ucezu Iwesibili ebizweni. La mabizo asetshenziswa efingqiwe; kanje: 
umntwana wami abantwana bakho umntwana wethu 
umntanami abantabakho umntanethu

13.5 Indaba 
13.5.1 Izinhlobo zezindaba 
Izindaba ezibhalwayo azifani zonke. Umehluko ubonakala kahle ngendlela okusuke kubhalwe ngayo leyo ndaba. 
Isihloko naso siyakwazi ukuveza ukuthi singesaluphi uhlobo lwendaba. Uma unikezwe isihloko, kufanele ukwazi ukusibona ukuthi sifuna ubhale kanjani. Ziningana izinhlotshana zezindaba ezilotshwayo. Noma-ke umngcele ungeke ubonakale kahle-hIe kwezinye, sizozama nokho ukuveza umehluko osobala ezindabeni. 
Ezindabeni ezejwayelekile singabala lezi zinhlobo ezilandelayo: elandisayo, echazayo, esangxoxo, neyokwethula umbiko. Uma kubhalwa indaba kudingeka kusheshe kubonakale ukuthi indaba leyo iluhlobo luni. Umehluko wezindaba uvela kalula esingenisweni. 
99 




107. 
108. 
109. 
110. 

Akesithi fahla ngomehluko okhona kulezi zinhlobo zezindaba. Indaba elandisayo indaba efuna uxoxe ngezigigaba nezehlakalo ezithile. Ubuciko bayo buvela kahle uma olobayo ekwazi ukulandelanisa izehlakalo ngendlela efanele. Akufanele nakancane izigigaba zixoveke noma zishayisane. Inhle indaba elandisayo uma oyilobayo izigigaba ezihlela ngokwenyuka kwazo. Le ndaba ifuna olobayo anamathele esihlokweni sendaba. Yikho lokho okusiza ukuba izehlakalo zingaxoveki. 

Indaba echazayo iyachaza noma yini leyo esesihlokweni. !fuoa umuntu okwazi kahle ukuchaza. Nakhona ekuchazeni kuba kuhle uma uqala ngasengxenyeni ethile, ugcine ngeuye ingxenye. Indaba echazayo elotshwe ngobuciko yenza ukuthi oyifundayo kube sengathi uyibona ngamehlo leyo nto echazwayo. Yindaba efuna amaqiniso lena. Oloba indaba echazayo kuhle abe nolwazi lokukhetha amagama achazayo. 

Ingxoxo yindaba yokuxoxisa noma eyimpikiswano yabantu ababili noma ngaphezulu. Imibono yalabo abaxoxiswayo yiyona ekhulisa indaba. Impikiswano leyo kuhle ibekwe ngezigatshana ukuze kwakbeke indaba. 

Indaba yokwethula umbiko indaba efana nokwethula amaminithi omhlangano. Le ndaba ifuna ubuciko nayo ngoba obekukhulunywa kuhle kuzwakale kahle kulowo ofunda indaba. 

13.5.2 Vika vakandini 

Bhala isiqeshana esinemigqa engeqile kweyisishiyagalombili ngomehluko phakathi kwendaba eyingxoxo nelandisayo.
