27.2 Ukusetshenziswa kolimi 
27.2.1 Ulimi oluselshenziswa emisebenzini elhile 

Ilowo nalowo msebenzi unolimi oluthile olusetshenziswa kuwona. Lolu limi luziwa kuphela yilabo abasebenza lowo msebenzi. Akuvumelekile ukuthi ulimi olusetshenziswa emsebenzini ulukhulume kubantu abangalwazi 1010 limi. Lolu limi Iwasemsebenzini luvama ukuxuba izilimi. 
1. Okubangela ukuxuba izilimi 
. (a) Ukuqondisa ngqo okukhulumayo 

Ukuxuba izilimi kwenza ukuba ungalokhu uthemeleza kepha ukusho ngqo osuke ufuna ukukusho. 
(b) Ukuswela amagama ozowasebenzisa 

Ukweswela amagama ongawasebenzisa esikhundleni segama elithile, kuyakwenza ukuba uxube izilimi. Isibonelo salokhu yilesi esilandelayo: Ngisayokwenza iExperiment. 
(c) Ukwenza kubelula ukukhuluma 

Sixuba izilimi ukuze senze kubelula ukukhuluma amagama amasha olimini. 

(d) Kwesinye isikhathi umuntu usebenzisa lolu limi oluxutshiwe ukuze kubonakale ukuthi ufundile nesiNgisi uyasazi.

27.3 Uhlelo 
.27.3.1 Ukusetshenziswa kwesenzo emshweni 
Isenzo sisetshenziswa kakhulu emshweni. Umusho ongenaso isenzo sengathi awuzwakali kahle noma ikhona imisho engenasenzo. Isenzo phela yisona esinikeza umqondo ophelele emshweni. Igama elilodwa nje eliyisenzo lingaba umusho ogcwele. 
Izibonelo Uyahamba Siyabusa Ufikile 
Emshweni ejwayelekile neqondile isenzo sisetshenziswa nomenzi nomenziwa. 
Ake sifunde Ie misho: 
Umfana uqhweba amadoda. Amadoda aphuza utshwala. Abantu babuka ukhamba. 
Kule misho engenhla amabizo asekuqaleni angomenzi kanti ekugcineni kwemisho kunomenziwa. 
Kukhona eminye imisho lapho izenzo zize zisebenze zimbili noma ngaphezulu. Le misho yalolu hlobo imisho embaxa. 
Ake sifunde lemisho: 
Ugaya utshwala ukuze aphuze. Ufuna ukhamba uzothela utshwala. Amadoda ayaphuza ukuze ajabule. 
Le misho njengoba inezenzo ezimbili kukhona umshwana oyinhloko nokhonzile. 
Isenzo emshweni singasetshenziswa nezinye sibe sendleleni engafani nasezinkathini ezahlukene.

27.5 Indaba 
27.5.1 Ukulolshwa kwencwadi yezimpahla 

Olunye uhlobo Iwezincwadi ezilotshwayo incwadi yokuthenga izimpahla. Lezi zincwadi zibangwa ukuthi kwesinye isikhathi asikwazi ukufinyelela kubathengisi. Indlela elula-ke yokuthintana nabathengisi eyokubalobela. 

Incwadi yokuthenga izimpahla ivama ukuba namakheli amabili. Phela Ie ncwadi ayifani nencwadi yomngani neyeziWobo, iyincwadi yomsebenzi, yingakho inamakheli amabili. Amakheli lawa abhalwa aqonde angatshekiswa. Elinye ikheli lisesandleni sokudla elinye lisesandleni sokunxele. Ikheli elisesandleni sokudla elalowo ongumbhali wencwadi. Leli kheli ligcina ngokuba kubhalwe usuku. Ikheli elibhalwa esandleni sokunxele elomnikazisitolo leso othenga kuso izimpahla. Aligcini-ke leli kheli ngosuku. 

Kule ncwadi-ke akubhalwa amanye amaxoxo ngaphandle kokufuna izimpahla kuphela. Isibingelelo sencwadi yokuthenga izimpahla siyisibingelelo esihloniphayo ngoba kwesinye isikhathi awazani nabantu labo othenga kubo. Isibingelelo singathi Mnumzane noma Banurnzane. Emva kwesibingelelo ulandelisa ngengxoxo efanele. Ucela usizo kubanikazi bezimpahla ukuba bakuthumelele izimpahla. Kuhle ubacele noma ubancenge, akusho lutho ukuthi uzozikhokhela izimpahla. Uma ufuna izimpahla zize ngeposi, chaza; uma ufuna bazilethe shono. 

Kulula ukubhala Ie ncwadi ngoba ikhuluma ngento eyodwa kuphela. Uma usubingelele wacela ukuposelwa izimpahla, uyazisho-ke izimpaWa ozifunayo. Izimpahla lezo kufuneka uzisho ngamagama futhi ubeke ubungako bazo. Zama ukuthi izimpahla ozifunayo zicace ukuthi yiziphi ukuze bakunikeze impahla okuyiyona obuyifuna. Loba wena lezi zimpahla zonke ziphelele. Ekuphetheni, loba isamba sonke semali neyokuposa.Esiphethweni sencwadi chaza ukuthi imali uyifakile lapho. Ekugcineni ubhala igama nesibongo.

27.6 Indaba emfishane 27.6.1 

1. Abalingiswa 

Abalingiswa bendaba emfishane kudingeka babembalwa. Kuba kuhle uma bebane noma ngapbansi kwalokho. Uma kwenzekile baba baningi, bangeqi kwabayisihlanu. Kudingeka ukuba laba balingiswa benze into emfishane isenzeko sabo singelulwa. Kudingeka kubekhona umlingiswa okwazi ukubonakala wonke amacala. Endabeni emfishime kuyenzeka kubekhona umlingiswa olele cu. Kufanele sibheke futhi ukuthi ukhona yini umlingiswa oqavile; umlamuli kanye nomqhathi. Isici noma ukhondolo lomli. ngiswa kudingeka ukuba kuvezwe kusasuka phansi ojena. Masingachazelwa kepha asibabone ngendlela abaziphethe ngayo, abenza ngayo abakucabangayo ngezigameko ezithile. Umfundi akazitholele yena ukhondolo kanye nokukhula komlingiswa ngaphandle kokuba atshelwe umlobi. 

2. Isingeniso sibe sifishane 

Isingeniso asibe sifishane sishaye emhlolweni. Ibinza lesingeniso lingaba linye kube yilona elidonsela umfundi ernzimbeni noma ezingxenyeni ezibalulekile zendaba. 

3. Ingxoxo mayibe umqondo owodwa 

Kudingeka ukuba indaba emfishane ibe nomqondo owodwa omfishane ohlaba umxhwele. Lo mqondo kudingeka ude uveza okwenzekayo okuyizinkinga kuze kuyofika ekugcineni. 

4. Indaba emfishane mayikhule ngokushesha 
Indaba emfishane ayikuvumeli ukuba. uthemeleze uchaze izinto eziningi. Ukukhula kohl aka lwayo kuze kufike kuvuthondaba kwenzeka ngokushesha. Lokhu kudala ukuba zishiywe. ngaphandle izinto ezingasemqoka endabeni. I1owo nalowo musho kudingeka ukuba ubesemqoka ekukhulisweni kwendikimba. Ukuze kugcizelelwe ukukhula ngokushesha kwendaba emfishane, kufanele umlobi akwenze kube kufishane ukuxoxwa kwezigameko. Kudingeka achaze anikeze inkulumompikiswano Y. emfishane, athinte kuphela isenzeko esisemqoka. Ukongiwa kwamagama kubaluleke kakhulu endabeni emfishane. 

218 

5 .. Uhlaka 

Umlobi akaluhlele uhlaka Iwendaba yakhe emfishane ngendlela yokuthi luhehe umfundi ukuba ayifunde indaba kuze kube sekugcineni. Konke okuxoxwayo kudingeka kuphathelane nendaba. Okuxoxwayo makubaluleke ekuqhubeni izigigaba ezenza uhlaka Iwendaba emfishane. Lezi zigigaba kudingeka zakheke zize zifike kuvuthondaba Iwendikimba yendaba. 
6. Uvulhondaba 

Lapha kusesicongweni sendaba emfishane. Lokho obekukade kuxake umlingiswa oqavile kufika ezingeni eliphezulu. Emva kovulhondaba indaba emfishane ayibe isakwazi ukuqhubeka, kepha kuye kulandele lokhu esikubiza ngokulhi ibohlololo. 
7. Ibohlololo 
Emva kovulhondaba indaba kudingeka ingabe isaqhubeka kakhulu kepha ayishiye umfundi ecabanga ngendikimba. 
8. Isiphelho 

Lapha-ke sekuthukululwa ifindo. Yilapho okuxazululwa khona i~king~ ebiy~lhulwe ng~kuqaleni kwendaba. Isiphetho nesingeDlSO slba slfishane slshaye emhlolweni. Kwesinye isikhalhi kungaba umusho oje kuphela. Isiphelho siza nento ethile ema. ngalisayo fulhi ebingalindelwe. Lokhu kubizwa ngokulhi ingwi. 
jikhwebu. 	.

27.7 Okudingeka ukuba kwenziwe 

Uthisha makaqedelise abafundi umsebenzi walelo sonto ongaqedwanga. Lokhu uyokuhlela futhi akwenze ngendlela eyovumelana naye kanye nabafundi. Uma esezenelisile ukuthi umsebenzi uwuqede ngempela, usengadlulela phambili. Kuyoba kuhle uma abafundi besawulandela kahle umsebenzi owenziwayo.

28.3 Uhlelo 
28.3.1 Isilandiso emshweni 

Sesike sathi fahlafahla ngokusetshenziswa kwesenzo emshweni. Uma isenzo sisetshenziswe emshweni sisibiza ngokuthi isilandiso. Isenzo esiyisilandiso sinezakhi zesenzo, izinsizasenzo, kanye 
	nezivumelwano. 	. 

Kwesinye isikhathi isilandiso siyasetshenziswa emshweni njengesibaluli. Uma sisetshenziswa njengesibaluli siphongozwa ngesivumelwano sesibaluli. . 
lzibonelo 

Umfana ohambayo .. Abantwana abalambayo. Ukuloba okungalungile. 

Isenzo uma sisetshenziswa njengesichasiso emshweni sisebenza' kanye nesivumelwano sikamenziwa. 
lzibonelo 

Umuntu engimbonayo. Izandla ongazigeziyo. Umuzi owakhayo. 

Ezinye izenzo ezisetshenziswa njengesichasiso zilandelwa iziqu zongumnini zoqobo. 
lzibonelo 

Umuntu othole inja yakhe. Ingane entshontshe uswidi wethu. Umfana olahle imali yakhe. 

Uma isenzo sisetshenziswe emshweni njengesibaluli, singakhombisa uhlelo oluvumayo nenkathi yamanje.

28.3.2 Vula amasango 

Chaza kabanzana izindlela okungasetshenziswa ngazo izenzo njengesichasiso. 

28.4 Awungiqabule ubuthongo 

Namhlanje bontanga sideka itafula silungisela ukuba kudliwe. Umfundisi makaqoke abathile ukuba basilinganisele ukuthi lidekwa kanjani itafula. Asiyibone imimese nezimfologo sekuhlezi sekulindele ukuba kuhlale umuntu akuthathe akusebenzise. 

Ngenkathi ulideka phela leli tafula kuhle ukuthi ube usitshela nangomlomo futhi ukuthi wenzani. Uma ubeka isitsha sesobho sitshele ukuthi isitsha sesobho lesi ngisibeka lapha. Laph~ ngibeka imfologo yona ihlala kanje, ummese wona uhlala lapha uqhubeke njalo uze uyoliqeda ukulideka. 
Sesifile ukuconsa amathe, awusidekele uliqede.

28.5 Indaba 
28.5.1 Incwadi yokududuza 	. 
Sesike saxoxa ngokulotshwa kwalohi hlobo Iwencwadi. Okusemqoka ngale ncwadi ukuthi kufanele iphumelele ukufeza umsebenzi wayo. Umuntu of un de incwadi kufanele nakanjani asale eduduzekile. 
Sizoke silobe enye yezincwadi eziduduza umuntu oshonelwe isihlobo sakhe.

Ngethemba uhambe kahle usuka emhlanganweni. Nokbo-ke sizwile izindaba ezimbi ezikuvelele. Siyadabuka kakhulu nawe siyakuzwela ngesihlobo sakbo. 
Noma kunjalo-ke yima isibindi njengendoda. Phela emhlabeni .• kukhona konke okuhle nokubi. Ungalahli ithemba ngoba usuvelelwe okubi. Kuzodlula masinyane ngoba nakwabanye kuyedlula. Cabanga ngekusasa ukbohlwe osekwenzekile. Ungabi nemidlinzo emibi, ngeke ikufikise ndawo. Emhlabeni vele thina bantu sifana nezivakashi nje. 
Sikufisela impilo enhle, uphumelele kukho konke okwenzayo. Sethemba uzolala ngenxeba. 
Bayakhonza bonke ekhaya. 
Yimina umzala wakho 
UMbaliza 
I.e ncwadi niyayibona ukuthi ayiphathi izingxoxo ezingahambela-, ni nokududuza. Oyifundayo futhi uyezwa ukuthi injongo yayo akusikho ukuvusa usizi. 
28.5.2 Vula amasango 
Bhala incwadi eya kumhlobo wakho odukelwe isihlobo sakhe ongasenathemba lokusithola.

28.6 Imibhalo 28.6.1 Iyini inkondlo 
Inkondlo iwuchungechunge Iwemicabango elakanyene eyenzelwe ukuchukuluza impendulo ethize kumfundi. I.e mpendulo umfundi azama ukuzinomfiyela yona, inesimo esifana naso esembongi ngenkathi iqamba yona inkondlo. Uma uhumusha inkondlo, ku- 
.' dingeka ueabange izincazelo. Kukhona izlnga lokuqala lapho inkondlo oyixoxa njengoba injalo kanye nezinga lesibili lapho okudingeka ukuba uthole khona incazelo yenkondlo efihlekile. 'Umfundi osezingeni eliphezulu ilowo okwazi ukufinyelela encazelweni ecashile yenkondlo aphinde futhi ajubalale ngezinye izincazelo. Kudingekaumfundi kumjabulise ukufunda inkondlo kubuye kumvusele amadlingozi ukuba naye abhale eyakhe. 
Inkondlo ingenye indicia yokusebenzisa ulimi. Inkondlo 'YlSlkhall esikhulu sokuthombulula okusezibilinini zabantu ngaphakathi. Ubunkondlo busolimini esilukhulumayo. Okubalulekile enkondlweni kuwukwethulwa komqondo ojiyile. UbunkoniIlo abukbo endleleni ehleleke ngayo kepha busengqikithini eeashlle. Inkondlo isingethwe ukunkondloza kwayo. Inkondlo isivezela imizwa nemicabango yembongi. Inkondlo i1ondoloza amasiko kimye nomlando wesizwe. Imbongi iye ibhale inkondlo ngenxa yokuhungulwa yizinto eziyizungezile. Imbongi isebenzisa amagama kanye nemisindo evezwa yila magama ukusibumbela isithombe esithile ezingqondweni zethu. Okwenza inkondlo ihluke kwemi. nye imibbalo ukuba nesalamuzi kwayo. Okunye okubalulekile ukuthi inkondlo ithandanisa amagama ngobungoti obuhambisana nesigqi esingatholakali kweminye imibhalo. Inkondlo iyisithombe sempilo esibekwe ngobuqiniso bangunaphakade. Inkondlo ingukuphelela okuphicayo okwenziwe izingxenyana ezahlukene kepha ezinobudlelwano esimweni sazo. Inkondlo iyizwi labaphansi elifika ngephupho usemhlabeni wabaphansi. Kwalani kuthi kwesikabhadakazi uzwe usunyenyezelwa izwi labaphansi. Lapho ukhahlela isiphuku siyolahleka laphaya, uvuke udwebe imidwa engeke iphele ukubhubha komhlaba kungakafiki.

29.6 Imibhalo 29.6.1 Izifengqo 
Akuzukukhulunywa ngazo zonke izifengqo lapha'. Kuzothathwa kuphela lezo ezimbalwa okuhlelwe ukuba zifundwe kuleli banga esikulo. 
Nazi lezi zifengqo: 
1. Isingathekiso 
Isingathekiso siyisifaniso esifinyeziwe. Izakhi zokufanisa njenga., .Cana., .nganga., kuhle., okwe., sa. njalonjalo ziyashiywa zingasetshenziswa. UmeWuko phakathi kwesingathekiso kanye nesifaniso ukuthi isifaniso sifanisa ngokuqondile kanti isingathekiso sona sifanisa ngokugudlisela. Akesibheke nasi isifaniso kanye nesingathekiso esilandelayo: 
Unenhliziyo efana neyebhubesi. - Isifaniso Unenhliziyo yebhubesi. - Isingathekiso 
Ezinye izibonelo zezingathekiso yilezi ezilandelayo: 
Wangithela ngezihlambi zezinyembezi. 
Izwi liyisibani ezinyaweni zami, nokukhanya endleleni yami. 
Amahubo 
(a) lsingathekiso esinwetshiwe 
Isibonelo sesingathekiso esinwetshiwe kungaba yilesi esilandelayo: Ensimini ebanzi yemfundo esingena kuyona, kunabafundi abaningi asebeqaIile ukufula ngamasikela abo. Isivuno sixhaphakile kangangokuthi umfuli okhetha izikhwebu budedengu futhi osabalala nensimu yonke angagcina efule amahhevu. 
(b) lsingathekiso esixubile 
Lesi singathekiso sihlanganisa emshweni owodwa izingathekiso ezimbili ezahlukene.

lsibonelo

30.1.1 Funda Ie ndaba bese uphendula imibuzo elandelayo 
Ukugenda 

Ukugenda lokhu umdlalo wamantombazane nabafana kodwa uthandwa kakhulu amantombazane. Kuyenzeka nabo abafana bathi uma belusile bese bewudlala 10 mdlalo wokugenda. 

Uma kuzogendwa kumbiwa isigojana esingashonile kakhulu ph ansi bese kufakwa khona amatshe amaningi. Abanye lamatshe bawabiza ngokuthi amagendo. Kuye kuthi phakathi kwala matshe kube yilowo nalowo ozodlala akhethe itshe elihle alithandayo okuyilona azolokhu eliphonsa phezulu elenqaka. Leli tshe libizwa ngokuthi ingendo. Uma-ke bonke abazodlala sebenazo izingendo, kuye kube sekuyaqalwa njalo sekuyadlalwa. 

Lo mdlalo wokugenda udlalwa ngokuthi kuphonswe ingendo phezulu bese isandla sikhipha amatshe emgodini ngenkathi ingendo isephezulu. Kufanele phela ithi ibuya ingendo ukwazi ukuyinqaka futhi ingaze iwele phansi. Emveni kokuyibamba kufanele amatshe uwaphindisele emgodini futhi kodwa kusale itshe elilodwa ngaphandle. Kuyaqhubeka-ke lokhu, ulokhu ushiya itshe elilodwa njalo ngaphandle, abe mabili, abe mathathu kuqhubeke njalo kuze kuyofika kwayisihlanu. Amatshe umuntu asewadlile uwabiza ngokuthi izinkomo zakhe. Uma kwenzeka esha lona odlalayo, kudlala omunye amatshe aze aphele emgodini.

1. Obani laba okuthiwa bakukhonze kakhulu ukugenda?

wokugenda?

4. Yini ingendo? 
5. Lo mdlalo wokugenda udlalelwa endlini noma phandle? 
Chaza ukuthi ukusho ngani lokho okushoyo. 
6. Udlalwa emini noma ebusuku wona 10 mdlalo? Chaza. 

6. Ukusha uma kugendwa kusho (ukwehluleka ukudlala, ukushiswa amatshe ngenkathi udlala, ukukhipha onke amatshe emgodini). Nginikeze impendulo elungile kulezi. 

6. Ukuqotha ingendo kusho (ukudlala itshe lokugcina usuwaqede onke, ukuyigaya, ukuyishayanisa namanye). Nginikeze impendulo elungile kulezi.

30.2 Kumnandi ukugenda 

Namhl.anje sixoxa ngemidlalo yentsha. Sixoxa noma ingayiphi nle tmtdlalo yentsha esiyaziyo. Kungaba imidlalo yasekwaluseni kube imidlalo yasezikoleni nemidlalo yasemakhaya nje jikelele: 

Slyaphefumuia sonke bontanga makungabibikho abasiqhuba ngan.'adolo. Makube yilowo nalowo axoxe ngemidlalo yentsha ayazlYo noma asake wezwa ngayo. Siyintsha sonke phela lapha, slOgasho kanjani pho ukuthi imidlalo yethu asiyazi. Awusikhinindele-ke ngale midlalo thina sizobeka indlebe. 
Masehlukane okwamanje sizobuye sihlangane futhi ngokuzayo. 
30.3 Indaba 
30.3.1 Okusemqoka ekulobeni indaba 

Noma sesifundile ngokulotshwa kwendaba, kukhona nokho izinto okufanele ziqashelwe uma uzoloba indaba. Yizo lezo zintoke ezingenza indaba yakho ibengconywana. 

Uma ninikezwe izihloko eziningana, khetha isihloko ozozwana naso masinyane. Qikelela ukuthi isihloko uyasizwa ukuthi sifunani nawe ube nolwazi olugcwele ngaso. Kungakusiza ukuthatha ISIhloko sento ongakwazi ukuyibona nangamehlo engqondo kalula. 

Indaba kufanele uyenzele amalungiselelo enele. Ungasuki ukhwele phezu kokuloba ungakayiqoqi imibono ozoyibeka ngaleso sihloko. Yakha uhlaka ulufundisise ukuze kubonakale ukuthi indaba yakho izohlangana. Zama ukuqaphela" ukuthi isingeniso sakho siyaphumelela ukuheba. Kwesinye isikhathi ungabhala izingeniso eziningana bese ukhetha isingeniso esiyisona esihlaba umxhwele. Qaphela ukuthi isingeniso sakho sibe sifushane kodwa sizwakale ingqikithi yaso. Umsebenzi wesingeniso ukuveza kancane lokho okuzoshiwo endabeni. Zama ukuthi isingeniso simthathe ofunda indaba ezwe enelukuluku lokufunda indaba yakho. 

Kusemqoka ukwakha izigatshana njalo uma uwloba indaba. Qaphela ukuthi izigatshana lezo zinomqondo owodwa ophele1e. Uma unweba izigatshana zakho yonke imisho, qaphela ukulhi inobudlelwano nomusho omkhulu. Sebenzisa izindlela eziningi 
238 

zokuqala izigatshana zakho ukuze indaba yakho ithandeke, ingabi nokuphindaphinda. Uma uloba izigatshana, ungaphindaphindi kodwa loba imiqondo ehlukahlukene. Loba izinto ezisemqoka uzishiye lezo ezingenamsebenzi endabeni. 

Ukuze indaba yakho ibe sezingeni eliphakeme, qala ngasengxenyeni elhile uye kwenye. Lokhu kusiza ukuba indaba yakho izwakale ikhuphuka. 
Loba isiphetho esizwakalayo nesikhombisayo ukuthi indaba isisemaphethelweni. 
30.3.2 Ayihlome! 
Loba isigatshana esingeqile emigqeni elishumi ngezinto okufanele ziqashelwe umuntu ozoloba indaba. 

30.4 Ukusetshenziswa kolimi 30.4.1 Ukuhlonipha 

Ukuhlonipha bekwenziwa abesifazane abaganile ukugwema inkulumo ethile. Ukusetshenziswa kwegama elithile kwesinye isikhathi kungathinta igama likababezala noma umamezala noma omunye womndeni. Lokhu kudala ukuba kusungulwe amagama okuhlonipha.

30.5.1 Ukuselshenziswa kwesandiso emshweni 
Isandiso siyasetshenziswa emshweni silandele isenzo. Lokhu kukhombisa ukuthi isandiso esisuselwe ebizweni singasetshenziswa nesenzo; kanje: 
Sigenda egcekeni. 
Akhiphe amatshe emgodini. Izinkomo zingena ezibayeni. 
Kukhona imisho ekhombisa ukuthi isandiso sendawo singaba umenzi emshweni. Uma isandiso singumenzi, silandelwa isenzo. 
lzibonelo 
Emgodini kungena izinkomo. Ekhaya ziyadlala izingane. Esitolo sibone abantu. 
Uma isandiso sendawo sisetshenziswe emshweni, silandelwa isakhi kwa-. Lokhu kwenzeka kulezo zandiso ezinesiqalo pha-. 
lzibonelo

lzibonelo

lzibonelo 
Bafike izolo abantu.

Kungcono ukubiza Ie ngxenye yomsebenzi ngokuthi imvumeIwano . kunokuthi. i~vumelwanosigcino. Lokbo kushiwo ngoba lb~ye lfake okumngl okungatholakali ngempela ekugcineni kwemlgqa yenkondlo. K~ye kubekbona imvumelwamo siqalo kanye nemvumelwano slgcmo yamalunga noma yegama eliphelele enkondlweni. Ifuzankamisa kanye nefanamsindo nakho siyasho. ukuthi kuwuhlobo oluthile Iwemvumelwano. Imvumelwano kwesinye isikhathi ingabizwa ngokuthiwa imvumelwano "a" nemvumelwano "b", njalonjalo. Imvumelwano iveza isigqi esithile enkondlweni lokhu okuyenza ukuba izwakale kahle uma isihaywa. Kuningi okungashlwo ngemvumelwano, nokho kwethenjwa ukuthi kuyosiza lokhu okuncane.

30.7 Okudingeka ukuba kwenziwe 
Uthisha makabukezise abafundi umsebenzi owenziwe kulelo sonto. Uthisha uyozihlelela yena indlela ayibona ukuthi Iyomlungela kanye nabafundi bakhe. Uthisha makazenelise ngelt.Jpela ~kuthi abafundi sebeyawazi umsebenzi. Phela man]ena seslya ngasekupheleni konyaka, ilowo nalowo makafunde ngokukhulu ukuzimisela.

Isahluko 31 
31.1 Isivivinyo somcabango 
31.1.1 Kule ndaba engezansi izinlo zonakele zixoveke zaphela. 
Zidinga ukulungiswa. Awulungise-ke sibone. 
Intombazane yathatha izinjobo zayo yabhinca yaphelela yase ilandelwa inkonyane ngemuva yaphuma. Yafika exhibeni yathatha umphonsanyoni wayo yabonda uphuthu. K wangena okungumfanyana kubhince isigege sakho kuhamba kuqhobonyeka. Le ntombazane. yaqhubeka nokuvuthela umlilo owawungavuthi kahle khona Ie eziko emsamo. Izimbiza nezinkamba zazihlezi endaweni yazo esininini samadoda. Kunomuntu owayequzwa izinja esithumbanjeni ngasemsamo. Indlu lena phela yayifulelwe ngothayela njengazo zonke izindlu zesiZulu. Laphaya ngasefasiteleni kwakunamaguma asitha umoya. Enye insika laphaya emsamo yayisithanda ukuguga ingasaqinile kahle.

31.3 Indaba 
31.3.1 Okusemqoka ekulolshweni kwezincwadi 
Sesifundile ngokulotshwa kwezincwadi. Ake sigcizelele Izmto ezisemqoka ekulotshweni kwezincwadi nalokho okungenza ukuthi uma uloba incwadi ibe sezingeni eliphakeme. 
245 
.} 






Incwadi ilotshwa ngokuthi kusetshenziswe amakheli. Qaphela ukuthi ikheli ulibhala ngendlela efanele. Ungalokothi ushiye ikheli lalowo obhalayo Iingenalo usuku okwabhalwa ngalo incwadi. Usuku, inyanga kubhalwa ngesiZulu. Izincwadi ezinye zinamakheli amabili. Kufanele wazi ukuthi yiziphi izincwadi ezidinga amakheli amabili nalezo ezidinga elilodwa. 
Isibingelelo sisemqoka endabeni ngoba abantu esibalobelayo ngeke babingelelwe ngendlela efanayo. Isibingelelo sibhalwa esandleni sokunxele. Ingxoxo iqala emva nje kwesibingelelo. Kufanele ingxoxo yencwadi uyilobe ngobuciko ukuze ifeze lesosidingo ebhalelwa sona. Incwadi yomzali kufanele yehluke kakhulu encwadini ebhalelwe umngani. Qaphela ukuthi incwadi oyibhalayo iluhlobo luni. Enye incwadi ifuna inkulumo eqondile kuphela engenawo amanye amaxoxo. Ezincwadini zomsebenzi awukwazi ukuxoxa enye into ngaphandle kwalokho okusemqoka. 
Incwadi nayo ifuna ukubhalwa ngolimi olumnandi olunongiwe. Khetha amagama afanele ozowasebenzisa ekulobeni incwadi 
'yakho. Zama ukusebenzisa imisho emifishane ukuze kusheshe kuzwakale okushoyo. Uma uloba incwadi yokuthenga ungayeki ukucacisa yonke into oyifunayo ibe sobala. 
Sebenzisa isiphetho esifanelene nencwadi oyibhalayo. Kuhle wazi ukuthi yiziphi izincwadi ezifuna igama nesibongo salowo obhalayo nalezo ezifuna igama kuphela. 
31.3.2 Gadla sibone! 
Awubalule zonke izinto okufanele zingasali uma uloba incwadi.

31.5.1 Ukuphika okungayindawo 
Isenzo siyasetshenziswa ekwakheni uhlelo oluphikayo noluvumayo. Isenzo uma sisohlelweni oluphikayo sisuke sisetshenziswe sisodwa emshweni. Kuyenzeka kwesinye isikhathi sakhe ukuphika okungujuqu. Lolu hlobo lokuphika, uhlobo Iwesakhiwo sesenzo nebizo eliseduze kwalo.

"

31.6 Imibhalo 31.6.1 Ibiriza 
Igama elithi ibinza lisho isigaba noma indimana yenkondlo. Lezi zigatshana uma sezihlanganiswe ndawonye zenza inkondlo.

221. 
222. 
Inkondlo ivama ukuba nemvumelwano emabinzeni ayo. Kuningi okubhekwa emabinzeni enkondlo. Kubhekwa ubude bemigqa, amalunga amagama kanye nobungako bemigqa esebinzeni. Kungabalulwa lezi zinhlobo zamabinza: 
1. Ibinza elinomugqa owodwa 
Alwandile ezinkondlweni zesiZulu ibinza eliwulolu hlobo. Izimbongi zesiZulu esezimnkantsha ubomvu ziyalusebenzisa 101u hlobo lwebinza zilubeka ngezindlela ezahlukene. Sithola ibinza eliwumugqa elivezwa njengokuphindaphinda okufana nokwamaculo esonto enkondlweni ka L T L Mabuya ethi Wen'uyazi eseqoqweni lezinkondlo okuthiwa lzinsungulo. 
Lo mugqa uthi: Uthando! Yek'usinga lothando! 
2. Ibinza elinemigqa emibili 
Leli binza livama ukwenziwa ngemigqa emibili. K wesinye isikhathi liba nemvumelwanosigcino. Isibonelo salolu hlobo lwebinza lutholakala ekupheleni kwenkondlo ka L T L Mabuya ethi Kuwena qhude ethathwe eqoqweni lezinkondlo lzinsungulo. Nanti leli binza: 
Khala Qhude likamenz' Usitshele! 
3. Ibinza elinemigqa emithathu 
Leli binza lakhiwa ngemigqa emithathu kuphela. Le migqa ingaba nemvumelwano noma ingabi nayo. Lolu hlobo lwebinza lutholakala enkondlweni ka L B Z Buthelezi ethi Sobabili Mntakwethu. Nanti leli binza: 
Cosololo emphefumulweni. Ngizwa ukutshuza kompe. Kulo mugqa nguwe kuphela. 
4. Ibinza elinemigqa emine 
Leli binza lakhiwa ngemigqa emine. Lolu hlobo luvamile ezinkondlweni zesiZulu. Isibonelo saleli binza sitholakala enkondlweni ka L T L Mabuya esihloko sayo sithi Ngithanda Ie ng~ma eseqoqweni lezinkondlo okuthiwa Uvivi lokusa. 
Ibinza lithi: 
Ngiyayithanda Ie mvunge yentakaso. 
Engibelesela ngingadeli ngenhlokomo. 
Ingivuse ngovivi lokusa ngigegetheke. Nangomgugu wemizwelo yogqozi njengomgadlela.

31.7 Okudingeka ukuba kwenziwe 
Uthisha makaqedelise abafundi umsebenzi walelo sonto ongaqedwanga. Uthisha uzozihlelela yena indlela engase ibelula yokwenza lokhu. Uma esenesiqiniseko sokuthi uphele ngempela umsebenzi obuwenziwa kulelo sonto, uthisha angaqhubekela phambili. 
252 
Isahluko 32 
32.1 Isivivinyo somc~iiango- - 
32.1.1 Funda Ie ndaba bese uphendula imibuzo elandelayo 
Ukugqabuka kwegoda 
K wathi emveni kokuba uDingane esethole umbiko wokuthi impi yakhe akuyihambeli kahle eNcome, wabe esethumela kumfowabo uMpande ukuthi amsize ngebutho elizoyosiza eNcome. UMpande wenqaba ukwenza lokhu. UDingane wathukuthela wagana unwabu uma ezwa ukuthi uMpande wenqabile ukumsiza. Wabe esecabanga isu lokugudluza uMpande. Uthe esuka lapho wabe esethumela umqeku wezithole kuMpande ukuba akleze. Kwakucushwe umgoga lapha wokuthi uzothi uyeza uzobonga lezi zinkomo uMpande, bese embulala uDingane. UMpande lapha wasizwa uNdlela kaSompisi owayeyinduna enkulu kaDingane owaphathisa umbiko laba ababeqhuba izinkomo wokuthi uMpande angalokothi athi uzobonga izinkomo lezo. Emveni kwalokho uMpande wathutha konke okungokwakhe wawelela esilungwini ukuyokhonza khona. 
Emveni kwalokhu yabe isibambene eyamadodana kaSenzangakhona, angoDingane noMpande. Le mpi yabambanela endaweni okuthiwa kuseMaqongqo yagcina seyaziwa ngokuthi impi yaseMaqongqo. 
Nakuba impi kaMpande yanqoba lapha, kwasiza ukuthi induna yempi kaDingane, uNdlela kaSompisi, wayikhipha ngokuyiguba kakhulu impi kaDingane. Okunye futhi okwanqobisa impi kaMpande lapha ukuthi wayesizwa nangamaQadasi. Iqhawe elikhulu likaDingane, umfokaNzuza elinguNozishada kaMaqhoboza, kuthiwa lagwaza kwaze kwababuhlungu iziphanga. Kwathi uma libona ukuthi iyeWulwa eyangakubo, lalahla phansi izikhali lathi abeze baligwaze life ngoba alikwazi ukubuswa umuntu onobuchoboka lona uMpande. Agagaza kaningi amanye amabutho ecabanga ukuthi mhlawumbe uwacuphele ugibe nje 'uNozishada. Ekugcineni baze bamgwaza waphangalala. Ukufa kukaNozishada kule mpi yaseMaqongqo siyakuthola ezibongweni

Kwaba wukwehlulwa kwayo njalo lokho impi kaDingane okwabe sekuwukuxabana kwafuthi phakathi kukaDingane noMpande.

32.2 Ulhela wayeka 

Kulesi sikhathi samanje bontanga sesifika emaphethelweni endlela . yethu ebisiyihamba kuleli banga. Kulokhu kwaqala unyaka besiyiciba Ie nsema egingqika lapha phambi kwethu. Mhlawumbe kungenzeka ukuthi nezinkande zethu sezize zanqindeka ngenxa yalokhu kuciba siphindelela. Masizame ukuzicija zibe yizinungu-ke futhi manje bontanga. Phela isigingqika ngenkani 

254 

enkulu njengoba sesilapha nje ifuna ukusidudulela emathukwini. Thina-ke masiphokophelele phezulu edala. Ukuba sed ala phela kusho ukuphumelela ekuhlolweni kwethu. 

Ekucijeni kwethu izinkande zethu masixoxe sibonisane ngakho konke esesikwenzile nesisazokwenza empilweni yethu. Singakhohlwa umfundisi wethu okunguyena obesediyela Ie nsema eyimfundo. 

Kuyobakuhle ukuthi siyicibe siyinembe sonke Ie nsema esho ukusiphonsa emathukwini. Uma sikwazile ukuyinemba sonke, sobe sesifuna ukuyoba sedala sonke ngothi Iwethu. Kusho impumelelo lokhu ekupheleni konyaka. 
Masiweleleni ebangeni elilandelayo sonke bontanga. Sohlangana ngonyaka ozayo futhi. 

32.3 Indaba 
32.3.1 Ukwakhiwa kwezigalshana 

Okunye okusemqoka endabeni ukwakhiwa kwezigatshana. Sike saphawula ukuthi izigatshana zakhiwa kanjani. Okusemqoka ukuthi izigatshana lezo imiqondo yazo ithelelane zemukelane. Yizona izigatshana ezikhombisa ukuthi indaba ixhumene noma chao Akufuneki kube khona. isigatshana esingahambelani nendaba. 

Isigatshana leso kuhle sibe nomqondo owodwa owethulwa ngumusho osekuqaleni. Yonke imisho elandelayo icacisa ikhanyise lowo mqondo. Ezigatshaneni ungasisebenzisa isibonelo. Qaphela nokho ukuthi isibonelo Ie so sihambelana ngqo nomqondo waleso sigatshana. 
Kuhle ukukhetha amagama afanele uma uloba indaba. Yiwona phela amagama enza ukuthi indaba yakho izwakale futhi icace. Zama ukusebenzisa lawo magama kuphela akhethwe ngobuchweheshe. Indaba ezwakala kahle yindaba elotshwe ngemisho emifushane. Izigatshana zakho uyakwazi ukuzenza ngconywama ngokukhipha amaganyana alulana. Ake sifunde lesi sigatshana kanye nalesi esingezansi kwaso sibone ukuthi zehluke kanjani. Safika esiteshini. Abantu baningi lapha. Nampa omama abadayisayo. Kukhona izinyama eziconsa amafutha. Bazamile nokho ukuthi ukudla kwabo kuconsise amathe. Basho ngengila abanye, basho abakuthengisayo nohlamvu Iwakhona. Abanye bawuhlabe inhlali. Sathi ukucabanga singazi ukuthi sizothengani. Phela umashayandawonye siyawuzwa awuzibekile phansi. 

255 




227. 
228.

32.5 Uhlelo 
32.5.1 Isakhiwo samagama 
Sesifundile ngezingcezu ezahlukehlukene zenkulumo. Uma sibheka izingcezu eziningi zikhombisa ukuthi zinezakhi ezahlukehlukene. Izakhi ezisemqoka sengathi yilezo ezingasekuqaleni. 
Uma ucezu sithi ibizo, sibona ngoba kukhona isakhi esiyisiqalo kulelo gama. Izingcezu eziningi zibonakala ngezivumelwano. Nazo izivumelwano lezi ziyizakhi ezingasekuqaleni emagameni. Izakhi njengoba umsebenzi wazo kungukwakha amagama, nazo ziyakhiwa. Uma uhlanganisa esinye isakhi nesinye, kwakheka isakhi. Indlela okwakhiwa ngayo izivumelwano zesiphawulo nesibaluli iyakufakaza lokhu:

omuesiezin- 

Amagama amaningi futhi siwasebenzisa emshweni. Amagama asetshenziswe emshweni kuyenzeka kwenzeke izinguquko ezingafani. Akhona amanye amagama esiwasebenzisa ngezindlela ezingejwayelekile. Okusemqoka ukuthi uma igama lisetshenziswe emshweni linikeze umqondo ophelele noma othile emshweni. 

Amagama amaningi akhiwa ngokuthi kuphongozwe emshweni. Izakhi eziphongozwayo ngakho zisemqoka ekwakheni amagama. 
Ake uzihlole ukuthi uyakwazi ukubona izingcezu zenkulumo nail 
32.5.2 Ciba kuyacilshwa!! 
Kule ndatshana kukhona amagama abhalwe ngokunzima. Abhale phansi lawo magama bese usho ukuthi awucezuluni. Sazithela kumama omkhuru. Uhlezi emnyango udla amadumbe. Isitsha esiluhlaza sesiyancipha impela. Amadumbe lawo awakhe uphakelwe umntanakhe. Izideku zamadumbe akazidli uzibuka ngeso lengulube azilahle emgqonyeni mum be. Akakhulumi uyahlafuna kuphela. 
32.6 Imibhalo 32.6.1 Isigigaba 

Isigigaba . kubuye kuthiwe isehlakalo enkondlweni. Isigigaba sivama ukutholakala ikakhulukazi ezinkondlweni ezibongela amaqhawe. Lezi zinkondlo zivama ukuqukatha izigigaba eziningi ezahlukene mayelana nempilo yamaqhawe nom lando wawo. Isigigaba sona siye sincwele kancane sithathe okukodwa emla. ndweni wempilo yeqhawe sichaze ngakho. Isigigaba singakwazi ukuba sizimele sodwa ngaphandle kokuba sithikanyezwe ezinye izigigaba ezitholakala ezibongweni. Ngamanye amazwi lapha isigigaba singaqukatha umqondo ophelele ngokwaso. Isigigaba singasho futhi ukuthi siyingxenye yendaba ehlukaniswe ngezigaba eziningi ezahlukene. 

Isigigaba siyatholakala futhi emdlalweni esusa usinga. Kule midlalo kuye kube nebalana njena elichaza isigigaba esisodwa. Ukubekwa kwesigigabaemdlalweni kudinga ikhono kanye nobunyoningco obuvelele. Isigigaba kubalulekile ukuthi noma singakwazi ukuzimela sodwa kepha sibe nokuxhumana nezinye
